Question #55 (ID: 705841)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]M=\frac{\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta-1}{\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta+1}[/math] এবং [math]N=\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{3}[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]N=\sqrt{3}[/math]
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]M^{2}-N^{2}=0[/math]
গ. [math]N=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math] এবং [math]0<\theta \leq 2 \pi[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math] এর সম্ভাব্য মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{N}=\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\cot \frac{\pi}{3}+\operatorname{cosec} \frac{\pi}{3}\left[\because \theta=\frac{\pi}{3}\right] \\=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}+\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}=\frac{3}{\sqrt{3}}=\sqrt{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
 হলে [math]\mathrm{N}=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]M=\frac{\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta-1}{\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta+1}[/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm{N}=\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]
এখন, [math]M=\frac{\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta-1}{\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta+1}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\operatorname{cosec} \theta(\cos \theta+1-\sin \theta)}{\operatorname{cosec} \theta(\cos \theta-1+\sin \theta)}=\frac{\cos \theta+1-\sin \theta}{\cos \theta+\sin \theta-1} \\=\frac{(\cos \theta+1-\sin \theta)(\cos \theta+\sin \theta+1)}{(\cos \theta+\sin \theta-1)(\cos \theta+\sin \theta+1)}=\frac{(\cos \theta+1)^{2}-\sin ^{2} \theta}{(\cos \theta+\sin \theta)^{2}-1^{2}} \\=\frac{\cos ^{2} \theta+2 \cos \theta+1-\sin ^{2} \theta}{\cos ^{2} \theta+\sin ^{2} \theta+2 \sin \theta \cos \theta-1}=\frac{\cos ^{2} \theta+2 \cos \theta+\cos ^{2} \theta}{1+2 \sin \theta \cos \theta-1} \\=\frac{2 \cos ^{2} \theta+2 \cos \theta}{2 \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta}=\frac{\cos \theta+1}{\sin \theta}=\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}+\frac{1}{\sin \theta}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta=N \therefore M=N[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow M^{2}=N^{2} \quad \therefore M^{2}-N^{2}=0[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]N=\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]
 [math]N=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 হলে [math]\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}+\frac{1}{\sin \theta}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \theta+1}{\sin \theta}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\\\Rightarrow \left(\frac{1+\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}\right)^{2}=\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\right)^{2}\\\Rightarrow \frac{(1+\cos \theta)^{2}}{\sin ^{2} \theta}=\frac{1}{3}\\\Rightarrow \frac{(1+\cos \theta)^{2}}{1-\cos ^{2} \theta}=\frac{1}{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{(1+\cos \theta)(1+\cos \theta)}{(1+\cos \theta)(1-\cos \theta)}=\frac{1}{3}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1+\cos \theta}{1-\cos \theta}=\frac{1}{3}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1+\cos \theta+1-\cos \theta}{1+\cos \theta-1+\cos \theta}=\frac{1+3}{1-3}\\\Rightarrow \frac{2}{2 \cos \theta}=\frac{4}{-2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos \theta}=-2 \\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=-\frac{1}{2} \\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=-\cos \frac{\pi}{3} \\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\cos \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)=\cos \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{3}\right) \\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\cos \frac{2 \pi}{3}=\cos \frac{4 \pi}{3} \\\therefore \theta=\frac{2 \pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}\end{array}[/math]
কিন্তু [math]\theta=\frac{4 \pi}{3}[/math]
 গ্রহণযোগ্য নয়।কেননা [math]\theta=\frac{4 \pi}{3}, \text { (i) }[/math]
 নং সমীকরণকে সিদ্ধ করে না।[math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান [math]\theta=\frac{2 \pi}{3} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #56 (ID: 705842)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: SB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\begin{array}{l}A=\operatorname{cosec} \theta \\B=\cot \theta \\C=\sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{15}+\sin ^{2} \frac{13 \pi}{30}+\sin ^{2} \frac{16 \pi}{15}+\sin ^{2} \frac{47 \pi}{30}\end{array}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]35^{\circ} 29^{\prime} 37^{\prime \prime}[/math] কে রেডিয়ানে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]C=\sec \frac{\pi}{3}.[/math]
গ. [math]3 A^{2}+3 B^{2}=5[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর যেখানে, [math]0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi .[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l}35^{\circ} 29^{\prime} 37^{\prime \prime}=35^{\circ}\left(29 \frac{37}{60}\right)^{\prime}=35^{\circ}\left(\frac{1777}{60}\right)^{\prime} \\=\left(35+\frac{1777}{60} \times \frac{1}{60}\right)^{\circ}=\left(\frac{127777}{3600}\right)^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{127777}{3600} \times \frac{\pi}{180}\right)[/math]
 রেডিয়ান [math]\left[\because 1^{\circ}=\frac{\pi^{c}}{180}\right][/math]
 [math]=0.6195[/math]
 রেডিয়ান (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\begin{aligned}C & =\sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{15}+\sin ^{2} \frac{13 \pi}{30}+\sin ^{2} \frac{16 \pi}{15}+\sin ^{2} \frac{47 \pi}{30} \\& =\sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{15}+\sin ^{2}\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\pi}{15}\right)+\sin ^{2}\left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{15}\right)+\sin ^{2}\left(\frac{3 \pi}{2}+\frac{\pi}{15}\right) \\& =\sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{15}+\cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{15}+\sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{15}+\cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{15} \\& =2\left(\sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{15}+\cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{15}\right)=2.1=2\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]=\sec \frac{\pi}{3}\left[\therefore \sec \frac{\pi}{3}=2\right] \therefore C=\sec \frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]B=\cot \theta[/math]
এখন, [math]3 A^{2}+3 B^{2}=5[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 3 \operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta+3 \cot ^{2} \theta=5 \Rightarrow \cot ^{2} \theta+\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta=\frac{5}{3} \\\cot ^{2} \theta+1+\cot ^{2} \theta=\frac{5}{3} \Rightarrow 2 \cot ^{2} \theta=\frac{5}{3}-1=\frac{2}{3} \\\Rightarrow \cot ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{3} \Rightarrow \cot \theta= \pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\cot \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 থেকে পাই, [math]\cot \theta=\cot \frac{\pi}{3}=\cot \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \theta=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}[\because 0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi)[/math]
আবার, [math]\cot \theta=\frac{-1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 থেকে পাই, [math]\cot \theta=\cot \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right), \cot \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{2 \pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3} \quad[\because 0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi][/math]
নির্দিষ্ট সীমা [math]0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi[/math]
 এর মধ্যে [math]\theta[/math]
 এর সম্ভাব্যমানসমূহ [math]\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{2 \pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #57 (ID: 705843)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: JB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P=\sin \theta, Q=\cos \theta[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{R}=\tan \theta[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{5 \pi}{13}[/math] কে ডিগ্রি, মিনিট ও সেকেন্ডে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. [math]8 P^{2}+5 Q^{2}=7[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]R= \pm \sqrt{2}[/math]
গ. [math]2 P^{2}+3 Q=0[/math] এবং [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] এর সম্ভাব্য মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{5 \pi}{13}=\left(\frac{5 \pi}{13} \times \frac{180}{\pi}\right)^{\circ}=\frac{900^{\circ}}{13}=69 \frac{3^{\circ}}{13}=69^{\circ}\left(\frac{3 \times 60}{13}\right)^{\prime} \\=69^{\circ}\left(13 \frac{11}{13}\right)^{\prime}=69^{\circ} 13^{\prime}\left(\frac{11 \times 60}{13}\right)^{\prime \prime}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=69^{\circ} 13^{\prime} 50.77^{\prime \prime}[/math]
 (প্রায়)[math]\therefore \frac{5 \pi}{13}[/math]
 রেডিয়ান [math]=69^{\circ} 13^{\prime} 50.77^{\prime \prime}[/math]
 (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]P=\sin \theta, Q=\cos \theta, R=\tan \theta[/math]
এবং [math]8 P^{2}+5 Q^{2}=7[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore 8 \sin ^{2} \theta+5 \cos ^{2} \theta=7 \Rightarrow 8\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)+5 \cos ^{2} \theta=7\\\Rightarrow 8-8 \cos ^{2} \theta+5 \cos ^{2} \theta=7 \Rightarrow 3 \cos ^{2} \theta=1\\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sec ^{2} \theta}=\frac{1}{3} \Rightarrow \sec ^{2} \theta=3\\\Rightarrow 1+\tan ^{2} \theta=3 \Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \theta=3-1=2\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta= \pm \sqrt{2} \quad \therefore R= \pm \sqrt{2}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]2 P^{2}+3 Q=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \theta+3 \cos \theta=0\\\Rightarrow 2\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)+3 \cos \theta=0\\\Rightarrow 2-2 \cos ^{2} \theta+3 \cos \theta=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2} \theta-3 \cos \theta-2=0[/math]
 [উভয়পক্ষকে (-1) দ্বারা গুণ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2} \theta-4 \cos \theta+\cos \theta-2=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \theta(\cos \theta-2)+1(\cos \theta-2)=0 \\\Rightarrow (2 \cos \theta+1)(\cos \theta-2)=0\end{array}[/math]
কিন্তু, [math]\cos \theta-2 
eq 0[/math]
 কেননা [math]-1 \leq \cos \theta \leq 1[/math]
অতএব, [math]2 \cos \theta+1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \cos \theta=-1 \\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=-\frac{1}{2}=-\cos \frac{\pi}{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\cos \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)=\cos \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [শর্তানুসারে [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]
][math]\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\cos \frac{2 \pi}{3}=\cos \frac{4 \pi}{3} \therefore \theta=\frac{2 \pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্দিষ্ট সীমার মধ্যে [math]\theta[/math]
 এর সম্ভাব্য মানসমূহ: [math]\frac{2 \pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #60 (ID: 705846)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: A.E.R.E School and College, Savar, Dhaka
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a \sin \theta-b \cos \theta=c[/math] যেখানে [math]a, b, c[/math] ধ্রুবক।

Options:
ক. [math]c=0[/math] হলে [math]\sec \theta[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]a \sin \theta+b \cos \theta=\pm \sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}.[/math]
গ. [math]a=1, b=-1[/math] এবং [math]c=\sqrt{2}[/math] হলে [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math] শর্তে সমীকরণটি সমাধান কর।


Correct Answer:

Question:
একটি পাহাড়ের উচ্চতা 8.848 কিলোমিটার। পাহাড়টির শীর্ষবিন্দু দূরবর্তী কোনো একটি স্থানে 2.25° কোণ উৎপন্ন করে। রতন সকাল 10টা 35 মিনিটে ঐ স্থান থেকে পাহাড়টি দেখার চেষ্টা করছিল।

Options:
ক. [math]\tan\left(\frac{7\pi}{6}\right)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. পাহাড় থেকে ঐ স্থানটির দূরত্ব নির্ণয় কর।
গ. উক্ত সময়ে ঘড়ির ঘন্টার কাঁটা ও মিনিটের কাঁটার অন্তর্গত কোণের মানকে রেডিয়ানে প্রকাশ কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\tan \left(\frac{7 \pi}{6}\right)=\tan \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\tan \frac{\pi}{6}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

 খ

মনে করি, AB পাহাড়টি পাদবিন্দু A থেকে r কিলোমিটার দূরে ০ বিন্দুতে 2.25° কোণ উৎপন্ন করে ৷ পাহাড়ের উচ্চতা,AB = চাপ S[math]\therefore[/math]
 AB = 8.848 কি.মি.।এখন, [math]S=r \theta \Rightarrow S=\text { r. } \frac{2.25 \times \pi}{180}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 8.848=r . \frac{2.25 \pi}{180} \therefore r=225.31[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 পাহাড় থেকে ঐ স্থানটির দূরত্ব 225.31 (প্রায়) কিলোমিটার। [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ
[Image]
আমরা জানি,ঘড়িতে সর্বমোট 12টি ঘণ্টার দাগ কাঁটা থাকে।[math]\therefore[/math]
 ঘণ্টার কাঁটার ক্ষেত্রে 12 ঘণ্টা কেন্দ্রে উৎপন্ন করে [math]=360^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math],,\quad ,, \quad,, 1 \quad ,, \quad ,, \quad ,, \quad ,, \quad \quad ,,[/math]
 [math]=\frac{360^{\circ}}{12}=30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math],,\quad ,, \quad,, 1[/math]
 মিনিট [math],, \quad ,, \quad ,, \quad ,, \quad \quad ,,[/math]
 [math]=\frac{30^{\circ}}{60}=0.5^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [ [math]\because[/math]
 1 ঘন্টা = 60 মি.][math]\therefore[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math],,\quad ,, \quad,, 35[/math]
 মিনিট [math],, \quad ,, \quad ,, \quad ,, \quad \quad ,,[/math]
 [math]=0.5 \times 35=17.5^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 সকাল 10:35 টায় ঘড়ির ঘণ্টার কাঁটা ও মিনিটের কাঁটার অন্তর্গত কোণ [math]=3 \times 30^{\circ}+17.5^{\circ}=90^{\circ}+17.5^{\circ}=107.5^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{107.5}{180} \times \pi=1.876[/math]
 (রেডিয়ান (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #82 (ID: 705820)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2016 | Boards:  | Tags: DB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]\sin (\alpha+\beta)+\cos (\alpha+\beta)[/math] এর মান কত?
খ. উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math](\sin\alpha-\cos\alpha)^2=1-2\sin\alpha.\cos\alpha.[/math]
গ. [math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=2[/math] হলে, [math]\alpha[/math] এর মান কত?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক
[Image]
চিত্রে থেকে পাই, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর [math]\angle \mathrm{A}=90^{\circ}[/math]
আমরা জানি,[math]\begin{array}{l}\angle A+\angle B+\angle C=180^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \alpha+\beta=180^{\circ}-\angle A \\\Rightarrow \alpha+\beta=180^{\circ}-90^{\circ} \\\therefore \alpha+\beta=90^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\sin (\alpha+\beta)+\cos (\alpha+\beta)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\sin 90^{\circ}+\cos 90^{\circ} \\=1+0 \\=1 \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ
[Image]
চিত্রানুসারে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{AC}=1 \\\mathrm{BC}=\sqrt{\mathrm{x}^{2}+1}\end{array}[/math]
যেহেতু, [math]\angle B A C=90^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \quad A B & =\sqrt{B C^{2}-A C^{2}} \\& =\sqrt{\left(\sqrt{x^{2}+1}\right)^{2}-1^{2}} \\& =\sqrt{\mathrm{x}^{2}+1-1} \\& =\sqrt{x^{2}} \\& =x\end{aligned}[/math]
এখন, [math]\sin \alpha=\frac{A C}{B C}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{x^{2}+1}}[/math]
 [math]\cos \alpha=\frac{A B}{B C}=\frac{x}{\sqrt{x^{2}+1}}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=(\sin \alpha-\cos \alpha)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{x^{2}+1}}-\frac{x}{\sqrt{x^{2}+1}}\right)^{2} \\=\left(\frac{1-x}{\sqrt{x^{2}+1}}\right)^{2} \\=\frac{(1-x)^{2}}{x^{2}+1}\end{array}[/math]
ডানপক্ষ [math]=1-2 \sin \alpha \cdot \cos \alpha[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=1-2 \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{x^{2}+1}} \cdot \frac{x}{\sqrt{x^{2}+1}} \\=1-\frac{2 x}{x^{2}+1} \\=\frac{x^{2}+1-2 x}{x^{2}+1} \\=\frac{1-2 x+x^{2}}{x^{2}+1} \\=\frac{(1-x)^{2}}{x^{2}+1}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad(\sin \alpha-\cos \alpha)^{2}=1-2 \sin \alpha \cdot \cos \alpha[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গচিত্র থেকে পাই, [math]\tan \alpha=\frac{A C}{A B}=\frac{1}{x}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \alpha=\frac{1}{x^{2}}[/math]
এখানে, [math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=2[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\tan ^{2} \alpha}+\tan ^{2} \alpha=2 \\\Rightarrow \frac{1+\tan ^{4} \alpha}{\tan ^{2} \alpha}=2 \\\Rightarrow \tan ^{4} \alpha+1=2 \tan ^{2} \alpha \\\Rightarrow \tan ^{4} \alpha-2 \tan ^{2} \alpha+1=0 \\\Rightarrow \left(\tan ^{2} \alpha\right)^{2}-2 \cdot \tan ^{2} \alpha \cdot 1+1^{2}=0 \\\Rightarrow \left(\tan ^{2} \alpha-1\right)^{2}=0 \\\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \alpha-1=0 \\\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \alpha=1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \alpha=1[\because \alpha[/math]
 সূক্ষ্মকোণ, তাই [math]\tan \alpha[/math]
 এর মান ধনাত্মক নিয়ে [math]][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \tan \alpha=\tan 45^{\circ}\\\therefore \alpha=45^{\circ} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #108 (ID: 705774)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]M=\sin \theta[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{N}=\cos \theta[/math]
ক) [math]\cos \left(\frac{-25 \pi}{3}\right)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ) [math]12 \mathrm{M}^{2}+23 \mathrm{~N}=22[/math] এবং [math]\frac{3 \pi}{2}<\theta<2 \pi[/math] হলে [math]\tan \theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ) [math]\frac{2}{\mathrm{~N}^{2}}+\frac{\mathrm{M}^{2}}{\mathrm{~N}^{2}}=3[/math] এবং [math]0<0<2%[/math] হলে ও এর মান নির্ণয় কর।

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\cos \left(-\frac{25 \pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(\frac{25 \pi}{3}\right)[\because \cos (-\theta)=\cos \theta][/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(\frac{24 \pi+\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(8 \pi+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)=\cos \left(16 \times \frac{\pi}{2}+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\pi}{3}=\frac{1}{2} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{M}=\sin \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm{N}=\cos \theta[/math]
আবার, [math]12 \mathrm{M}^{2}+23 \mathrm{~N}=22[/math]
বা, [math]12 \sin ^{2} \theta+23 \cos \theta=22[/math]
বা, [math]12\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)+23 \cos \theta-22=0[/math]
বা, [math]12-12 \cos ^{2} \theta+23 \cos \theta-22=0[/math]
বা, [math]12 \cos ^{2} \theta-23 \cos \theta+10=0[/math]
বা, [math]12 \cos ^{2} \theta-15 \cos \theta-8 \cos \theta+10=0[/math]
বা, [math]3 \cos \theta(4 \cos \theta-5)-2(4 \cos \theta-5)=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore(4 \cos \theta-5)(3 \cos \theta-2)=0[/math]
হয়, [math]4 \cos \theta-5=0[/math]
বা, [math]\cos \theta=\frac{5}{4},[/math]
 য যা গ্রহণযোগ্য নয়, কারণ [math]- 1 ≤ cose ≤ 11[/math]

[Image]
অথবা, [math]3 \cos \theta-2=0[/math]
বা, [math]\cos \theta=\frac{2}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \theta=-\frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}\left[\because \frac{3 \pi}{2}গপ্রদত্ত রাশি, [math]\frac{2}{\mathrm{~N}^{2}}+\frac{\mathrm{M}^{2}}{\mathrm{~N}^{2}}=3[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{2+M^{2}}{N^{2}}=3[/math]
বা, [math]2+\mathrm{M}^{2}=3 \mathrm{~N}^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]2+\sin ^{2} \theta=3 \cos ^{2} \theta[/math]
বা, [math]2+\sin ^{2} \theta=3-3 \sin ^{2} \theta[/math]
বা, [math]4 \sin ^{2} \theta=1[/math]
বা, [math]\sin ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta= \pm \frac{1}{2}[/math]
ধনাত্মক মান নিয়ে পাই,[math]\sin \theta=\frac{1}{2}=\sin \frac{\pi}{6}=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{6}=\sin \frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
ঋণাত্মক মান নিয়ে পাই,[math]\sin \theta=-\frac{1}{2}=-\sin \frac{\pi}{6}=\sin \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\sin \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=\sin \frac{7 \pi}{6}=\sin \frac{11 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6}\therefore \theta=\frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #109 (ID: 705775)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: DiB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{(i) } \tan \alpha+\sec \alpha=A\\\text{(ii) } \mathrm{F}(\alpha)=\cos \alpha\end{array}[/math]
ক) [math]\cos \beta=\frac{2}{\sqrt{7}}[/math] হলে, [math]\cot \beta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ) [math]F\left(\frac{5 \pi}{2}-\alpha\right)=\frac{y^{2}-1}{y^{2}+1}[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathbf{y}^{2}-\mathbf{A}^{\mathbf{2}}=0[/math]
গ) [math]A=\sqrt{3}[/math] হলে, [math]\alpha[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর। যখন [math]0 \leq \alpha \leq 2 \pi[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\cos \beta=\frac{2}{\sqrt{7}}[/math]
আমরা জানি, [math]\sin \beta= \pm \sqrt{1-\cos ^{2} \beta}[/math]
 [math]\sin \beta= \pm \sqrt{1-\cos ^{2} \beta}[/math]
 [math]= \pm \sqrt{1-\left(\frac{2}{\sqrt{7}}\right)^{2}}= \pm \sqrt{1-\frac{4}{7}}= \pm \sqrt{\frac{7-4}{7}}= \pm \frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{7}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cot \beta=\frac{\cos \beta}{\sin \beta}=\frac{\frac{2}{\sqrt{7}}}{ \pm \frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{7}}}= \pm \frac{2}{\sqrt{3}} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\tan \alpha+\sec \alpha=\mathrm{A}[/math]
এবং [math]\mathrm{F}(\alpha)=\cos \alpha[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{F}\left(\frac{5 \pi}{2}-\alpha\right)=\cos \left(\frac{5 \pi}{2}-\alpha\right)=\sin \alpha[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{F}\left(\frac{5 \pi}{2}-\alpha\right)=\frac{\mathrm{y}^{2}-1}{\mathrm{y}^{2}+1}[/math]
 হলে[math]\sin \alpha=\frac{y^{2}-1}{y^{2}+1}[/math]
 বা [math]\frac{1}{\sin \alpha}=\frac{y^{2}+1}{y^{2}-1}[/math]
বা , [math]\frac{1+\sin \alpha}{1-\sin \alpha}=\frac{y^{2}+1+y^{2}-1}{y^{2}+1-y^{2}+1}=\frac{2 y^{2}}{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\text {} \frac{1+\sin \alpha}{1-\sin \alpha}=y^{2}[/math]
 বা [math]\frac{\frac{1+\sin \alpha}{\cos \alpha}}{\frac{1-\sin \alpha}{\cos \alpha}}=y^{2}[/math]
 বা [math]\frac{\sec \alpha+\tan \alpha}{\sec \alpha-\tan \alpha}=y^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{(\sec \alpha+\tan \alpha)(\sec \alpha+\tan \alpha)}{(\sec \alpha-\tan \alpha)(\sec \alpha+\tan \alpha)}=y^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{(\sec \alpha+\tan \alpha)^{2}}{\sec ^{2} \alpha-\tan ^{2} \alpha}=y^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{\mathrm{A}^{2}}{1}=\mathrm{y}^{2}[\because \sec \alpha+\tan \alpha=\mathrm{A}][/math]
বা, [math]\mathrm{y}^{2}=\mathrm{A}^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\therefore \mathrm{y}^{2}-\mathrm{A}^{2}=0[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\sec \alpha+\tan \alpha[/math]
 এবং [math]A=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sec \alpha+\tan \alpha=\sqrt{3}[/math]
বা, [math]\sec \alpha=\sqrt{3}-\tan \alpha[/math]
বা, [math]\sec ^{2} \alpha=(\sqrt{3}-\tan \alpha)^{2}[/math]
[বর্গ করে]বা, [math]1+\tan ^{2} \alpha=3-2 \sqrt{3} \tan \alpha+\tan ^{2} \alpha[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sqrt{3} \tan \alpha=3+\tan ^{2} \alpha-1-\tan ^{2} \alpha[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sqrt{3} \tan \alpha=3+\tan ^{2} \alpha-1-\tan ^{2} \alpha[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sqrt{3} \tan \alpha=2[/math]
 বা, [math]\tan \alpha=\frac{2}{2 \sqrt{3}}[/math]
 বা, [math]\tan \alpha=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \alpha=\tan \frac{\pi}{6}=\tan \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[\because 0 \leq \alpha \leq 2 \pi][/math]
বা, [math]\alpha=\frac{7 \pi}{6}[/math]
 গ্রহণযোগ্য নয়। কারণ [math]\alpha=\frac{7 \pi}{6} \text {. }[/math]
 এর জন্য প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটি সিদ্ধ হয় না।[math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয়' মান [math]\alpha=\frac{\pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #110 (ID: 705776)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A}=\sec \theta+\tan \theta[/math] এবং [math]B=\sec \theta-\tan \theta[/math]
ক) [math]\tan \left(-\frac{25 \pi}{6}\right)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ) প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{A-.1}{1-B}=\frac{\cos \theta}{1-\sin \theta}[/math]
গ) [math]B=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math] এবং [math]0<\theta<\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\tan \left(-\frac{25 \pi}{6}\right)=-\tan \frac{25 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]=-\tan \left(4 \pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]=-\tan \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\sec \theta+\tan \theta, B=\sec \theta-\tan \theta[/math]
বামপক্ষ, [math]=\frac{A-1}{1-B}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sec \theta+\tan \theta-1}{1-\sec \theta+\tan \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sec \theta+\tan \theta-\left(\sec ^{2} \theta-\tan ^{2} \theta\right)}{1-\sec \theta+\tan \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sec \theta+\tan \theta-(\sec \theta+\tan \theta)(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)}{1-\sec \theta+\tan \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{(\sec \theta+\tan \theta)(1-\sec \theta+\tan \theta)}{1-\sec \theta+\tan \theta}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\sec \theta+\tan \theta \\=\frac{1}{\cos \theta}+\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{(1+\sin \theta)(1-\sin \theta)}{\cos \theta(1-\sin \theta)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\sin ^{2} \theta}{\cos \theta(1-\sin \theta)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos ^{2} \theta}{\cos \theta(1-\sin \theta)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos \theta}{1-\sin \theta}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{A-1}{1-B}=\frac{\cos \theta}{1-\sin \theta}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]B=\sec \theta-\tan \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]B=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sec \theta-\tan \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1}{\cos \theta}-\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1-\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{3} \sin \theta=\cos \theta[/math]
বা, [math](\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{3} \sin \theta)^{2}=(\cos \theta)^{2}[/math]
 [উভয়পক্ষকে বর্গ করে)বা, [math]3+3 \sin ^{2} \theta-6 \sin \theta=\cos ^{2} \theta[/math]
বা, [math]3+3 \sin ^{2} \theta-6 \sin \theta=1-\sin ^{2} \theta \quad,\left[\because \sin ^{2} \theta+\cos ^{2} \theta=1\right][/math]
বা, [math]3 \sin ^{2} \theta+\sin ^{2} \theta-6 \sin \theta+3-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]4 \sin ^{2} \theta-6 \sin \theta+2=0[/math]
বা, [math]2\left(2 \sin ^{2} \theta-3 \sin \theta+1\right)=0[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sin ^{2} \theta-3 \sin \theta+1=0[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sin ^{2} \theta-2 \sin \theta-\sin \theta+1=0[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sin ^{2} \theta-2 \sin \theta-\sin \theta+1=0[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sin \theta(\sin \theta-1)-1(\sin \theta-1)=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore(\sin \theta-1)(2 \sin \theta-1)=0[/math]
হয়, [math]\sin \theta-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=1[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
অথবা, [math]2 \sin \theta-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
কিন্তু [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 গ্রহণযোগ্য নয়, কারণ [math]0<\theta<\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta[/math]
 এর মান [math]\frac{\pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #111 (ID: 705777)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{a}=\sec \theta-\tan \theta[/math] যেখানে [math]0<\theta<\frac{\pi}{2} .[/math]
ক) [math]10[/math] সে.মি. ব্যাসবিশিষ্ট বৃত্তের যে চাপ কেন্দ্রে [math]32°[/math] কোণ উৎপন্ন করে, তার দৈর্ঘ্য নির্ণয় কর।
খ) প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta=\frac{1-\mathrm{a}}{1+\mathrm{a}}[/math]
গ) [math]a=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কবৃত্তের ব্যাস = 10 সে.মি.[math]\therefore[/math]
 ব্যাসার্ধ, [math]r=\frac{10}{2}[/math]
 সে.মি. = 5 সে.মি.উৎপন্ন কোণ, [math]\theta=32^{\circ}=32 \times \frac{\pi}{180}[/math]
 রেডিয়ান[math]= 0.5585[/math]
 রেডিয়ান[math]\therefore[/math]
 চাপের দৈর্ঘ্য [math]\mathrm{s}=\mathrm{r} \theta=5 \times 0.5585[/math]
 [math]= 2.7925[/math]
 সে.মি. (Ans.)[math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]a=\sec \theta-\tan \theta[/math]
ডানপক্ষ = [math]=\frac{1-\mathrm{a}}{1+\mathrm{a}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)}{1+(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\sec \theta+\tan \theta}{1+\sec \theta-\tan \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\frac{1}{\cos \theta}+\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}}{1+\frac{1}{\cos \theta}-\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{1}{\cos \theta}(\cos \theta-1+\sin \theta)}{\frac{1}{\cos \theta}(\cos \theta+1-\sin \theta)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos \theta-1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta+1-\sin \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin \theta(\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta+1)}{\sin \theta(\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta-1)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)}{\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta-1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\left(\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta-\cot ^{2} \theta\right)-(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)}{\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta-1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)(\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta-1)}{(\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta-1)}[/math]
 [math]=\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta=[/math]
 বামপক্ষ[math]\therefore \operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta=\frac{1-a}{1+a}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]a=\sec \theta-\tan \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]a=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\sec \theta-\tan \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\sqrt{3} \sec \theta-\sqrt{3} \tan \theta=1[/math]
বা, [math](\sqrt{3} \sec \theta)^{2}=(1+\sqrt{3} \tan \theta)^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]3 \sec ^{2} \theta=1+2 \sqrt{3} \tan \theta+3 \tan ^{2} \theta[/math]
বা, [math]3+3 \tan ^{2} \theta=1+2 \sqrt{3} \tan \theta+3 \tan ^{2} \theta\left[\because \sec ^{2} \theta=1+\tan ^{2} \theta\right][/math]
বা, [math]-2 \sqrt{3} \tan \theta=2[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}=\tan \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question:
[math]A=7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3 \cos ^{2} \theta[/math] [math]B=15 \cos ^{2} \alpha+2 \sin \alpha[/math] যখন [math]-\frac{\pi}{2}<\alpha<\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
ক) [math]1.532[/math] রেডিয়ানকে ডিগ্রিতে প্রকাশ কর।
খ) [math]A = 4[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]-\frac{\pi}{2}<\alpha<\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
গ) [math]\alpha[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত কোণ [math]= 1.532^C[/math]
 [math]=\left(1.532 \times \frac{180}{\pi}\right)^{\circ}[\because 1[/math]
 রেডিয়ান [math]=\frac{180^{\circ}}{\pi}[/math]
 [math]= 87.78°[/math]
 [math]= 87° (0.78 x 60)'[/math]
 [math]= 87°46.8′[/math]
 [math]= 87°46′ (0.8 \times 60)"[/math]
 [math]= 87°46′48" (Ans.)[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3 \cos ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]A = 4[/math]
 হলে, [math]7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3 \cos ^{2} \theta=4[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3 \cos ^{2} \theta}{\cos ^{2} \theta}=\frac{4}{\cos ^{2} \theta}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{7 \sin ^{2} \theta}{\cos ^{2} \theta}+\frac{3 \cos ^{2} \theta}{\cos ^{2} \theta}=4 \times \frac{1}{\cos ^{2} \theta}[/math]
বা, [math]7 \tan ^{2} \theta+3=4 \sec ^{2} \theta[/math]
বা, [math]7 \tan ^{2} \theta+3=4\left(1+\tan ^{2} \theta\right)[/math]
বা, [math]7 \tan ^{2} \theta-4 \tan ^{2} \theta=4-3[/math]
বা, [math]3 \tan ^{2} \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\tan ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{3}[/math]
 ( দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গবিশেষ দ্রষ্টব্য: প্রশ্নটির তথ্য অসম্পূর্ণ। তাই প্রশ্নে [math]B = 7[/math]
 বিবেচনা করে [math]\alpha, \tan \alpha[/math]
, এবং [math]\cot \alpha[/math]
 এর মান নিচে নির্ণয় করে দেখানো হলো।দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathbf{B}=15 \cos ^{2} \alpha+2 \sin \alpha[/math]
 [math]B = 7[/math]
 হলে [math]15 \cos ^{2} \alpha+2 \sin \alpha=7 ;\left[-\frac{\pi}{2}<\dot{\alpha}<\frac{\pi}{2}\right][/math]
বা, [math]15\left(1-\sin ^{2} \alpha\right)+2 \sin \alpha=7[/math]
বা, [math]15 \sin ^{2} \alpha-2 \sin \alpha-8=0[/math]
বা, [math]15 \sin ^{2} \alpha-12 \sin \alpha+10 \sin \alpha-8=0[/math]
বা, [math]3 \sin \alpha(5 \sin \alpha-4)+2(5 \sin \alpha-4)=0 .[/math]
 [math]\therefore(5 \sin \alpha-4)(3 \sin \alpha+2)=0[/math]
হয়, [math]5 sina-4=0[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \alpha=\frac{4}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \alpha=\sin ^{-1} \frac{4}{5}=53.13^{\circ}[/math]
অথবা, [math]3 sina +2=0[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \alpha=-\frac{2}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \alpha=\sin ^{-1}\left(-\frac{2}{3}\right)=-41.81^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\sin \alpha[/math]
 এর উভয় মান গ্রহণযোগ্য। কেননা, [math]-\frac{\pi}{2}<\alpha<\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
আবার, একই কারণে $$ এর শুধু ধনাত্মক মান গ্রহণযোগ্য।[math]\therefore \sin \alpha=\frac{4}{5}[/math]
 হলে, [math]\cos \alpha=\sqrt{1-\left(\frac{4}{5}\right)^{2}}=\sqrt{1-\frac{16}{25}}=\sqrt{\frac{9}{25}}=\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 [math]\sin \alpha=-\frac{2}{3}[/math]
 হলে, [math]\cos \alpha=\sqrt{1-\left(-\frac{2}{3}\right)^{2}}=\sqrt{1-\frac{4}{9}}=\sqrt{\frac{5}{9}}=\frac{\sqrt{5}}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \alpha=\frac{\sin \alpha}{\cos \alpha}=\frac{\frac{5}{5}}{\frac{3}{5}}[/math]
 [যখন [math]\sin \alpha=\frac{4}{5}][/math]
 [math]=\frac{4}{5} \times \frac{5}{3}=\frac{4}{3}[/math]
এবং [math]\cot \alpha=\frac{1}{\tan \alpha}=\frac{1}{\frac{4}{3}}=\frac{3}{4}[/math]
আবার, [math]\tan \alpha=\frac{\sin \alpha}{\cos \alpha}=\frac{-\frac{2}{3}}{\frac{\sqrt{5}}{3}}[/math]
 [যখন [math]\left.\sin \alpha=-\frac{2}{3}\right][/math]
 [math]=-\frac{2}{3} \times \frac{3}{\sqrt{5}}=-\frac{2}{\sqrt{5}}[/math]
এবং, [math]\cot \alpha=\frac{1}{\tan \alpha}=\frac{1}{-\frac{2}{\sqrt{5}}}=-\frac{\sqrt{5}}{2} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #113 (ID: 705779)

Question:
[math]\mathrm{x}=\sin \theta[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{y}=\cos \theta[/math]
ক) দেখাও যে, [math]\operatorname{cosec}^{4} \theta-\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta=\cot ^{4} \theta+\cot ^{2} \theta[/math]
খ) [math]15 x^{2}+2 y=7[/math] এবং [math]-\frac{\pi}{2}<\theta<\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] [math]\tan \theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ) [math]2\left(y^{2}-x^{2}\right)-1=0[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর; [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কবামপক্ষ = [math]=\operatorname{cosec}^{4} \theta-\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]=\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta\left(\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta-1\right)[/math]
 [math]=\left(1+\cot ^{2} \theta\right) \cot ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]=\cot ^{4} \theta+\cot ^{2} \theta[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \operatorname{cosec}^{4} \theta-\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta=\cot ^{4} \theta+\cot ^{2} \theta[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]x=\sin \theta, y=\cos \theta[/math]
এবং [math]15 x^{2}+2 y=7[/math]
বা, [math]15 \sin ^{2} \theta+2 \cos \theta=7[/math]
বা, [math]15\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)+2 \cos \theta-7=0[/math]
বা, [math]15-15 \cos ^{2} \theta+2 \cos \theta-7=0[/math]
বা, [math]15 \cos ^{2} \theta-2 \cos \theta-8=0[/math]
বা, [math]15 \cos ^{2} \theta-12 \cos \theta+10 \cos \theta-8=015 \cos ^{2} \theta-12 \cos \theta+10 \cos \theta-8=0[/math]
বা, [math]3 \cos \theta(5 \cos \theta-4)+2(5 \cos \theta-4)=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore(5 \cos \theta-4)(3 \cos \theta+2)=0[/math]
হয়, [math]5 \cos \theta-4=0[/math]
বা, [math]\cos \theta=\frac{4}{5}[/math]
 [math]\cos \theta=\frac{4}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \theta= \pm \frac{3}{5} \quad\left[\because-\frac{\pi}{2}গদেওয়া আছে, [math]x=\sin \theta[/math]
 ও [math]y=\cos \theta[/math]
এবং [math]2\left(y^{2}-x^{2}\right)-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]2\left(\cos ^{2} \theta-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]2\left(\cos ^{2} \theta-1+\cos ^{2} \theta\right)-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]2\left(2 \cdot \cos ^{2} \theta-1\right)-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]4 \cos ^{2} \theta-2=1[/math]
বা, [math]4 \cos ^{2} \theta=3[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \theta= \pm \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
(+) চিহ্ন নিয়ে,[math]\cos \theta=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\cos \frac{\pi}{6}=\cos \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{1.1 \pi}{6}[/math]
(-) চিহ্ন নিয়ে,[math]\cos \theta=\frac{-\sqrt{3}}{2}=-\cos \frac{\pi}{6}=\cos \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\cos \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{5 \pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান, [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #114 (ID: 705780)

Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: SB

Question:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{(i) } 2 \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\mathrm{D}\right)=\sqrt{3}\\\text{(ii) } \tan ^{2} \theta+\cot ^{2} \theta-\frac{10}{3}=0 \text{.}\end{array}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]-1465^{\circ}[/math] কোণটি কোন চতুর্ভাগে অবস্থিত তা চিত্রসহ নির্ণয় কর।
খ. (i) নং এর সাহায্যে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]3 \sin D-4 \sin ^{3} D-\sin 3 D=0.[/math]
গ. (ii) নং হতে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর; যেখানে [math]0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক
[Image]
প্রদত্ত কোন [math]=-1465^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=-1440^{\circ}-25^{\circ} \\=-16 \times 90^{\circ}-25^{\circ} \\=-4 \times 360^{\circ}-25^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
অর্থাৎ, কোণটি চতুর্থ চতুর্ভাগে অবস্থিত। [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]2 \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-D\right)=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin D=\sqrt{3} \Rightarrow \sin D=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \mathrm{D}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\sin 60^{\circ} \therefore \mathrm{D}=60^{\circ}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=3 \sin D-4 \sin ^{3} D-\sin 3 D[/math]
 [math]=3 \times \sin 60^{\circ}-4\left(\sin 60^{\circ}\right)^{3}-\sin \left(3 \times 60^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [মান বসিয়ে][math]\begin{array}{l}=3 \times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}-4\left(\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right)^{3}-\sin 180^{\circ} ;\\=\frac{3 \sqrt{3}}{2}-4 \times \frac{3 \sqrt{3}}{8}-0=\frac{3 \sqrt{3}}{2}-\frac{3 \sqrt{3}}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=0=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore 3 \sin D-4 \sin ^{3} D-\sin 3 D=0[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,[math]\tan ^{2} \theta+\cot ^{2} \theta-\frac{10}{3}=0 ; 0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \theta+\frac{1}{\tan ^{2} \theta}=\frac{10}{3}\\\Rightarrow \frac{\tan ^{4} \theta+1}{\tan ^{2} \theta}=\frac{10}{3}\\\Rightarrow 3 \tan ^{4} \theta+3-10 \tan ^{2} \theta=0\\\Rightarrow 3 \tan ^{4} \theta-9 \tan ^{2} \theta-\tan ^{2} \theta+3=0\\\Rightarrow 3 \tan ^{2} \theta\left(\tan ^{2} \theta-3\right)-1\left(\tan ^{2} \theta-3\right)=0\\\Rightarrow \left(\tan ^{2} \theta-3\right)\left(3 \tan ^{2} \theta-1\right)=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 হয়, [math]\tan ^{2} \theta-3=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \theta=3\\\Rightarrow \tan \theta= \pm \sqrt{3}\end{array}[/math]
‘+' চিহ্ন দিয়ে, [math]\tan \theta=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\sqrt{3}=\tan \frac{\pi}{3}=\tan \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)\\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\tan \frac{\pi}{3}=\tan \frac{4 \pi}{3} \therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}\end{array}[/math]
‘–' চিহ্ন নিয়ে, [math]\tan \theta=-\sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \tan \theta=-\sqrt{3}=\tan \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)=\tan \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right) \\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\tan \frac{2 \pi}{3}=\tan \frac{5 \pi}{3} \therefore \theta=\frac{2 \pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3}\end{array}[/math]
আবার, [math]3 \tan ^{2} \theta-1=0 \Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{3} \Rightarrow \tan \theta= \pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
‘+' চিহ্ন নিয়ে, [math]\therefore \tan \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \Rightarrow \tan \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}=\tan \frac{\pi}{6}=\tan \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\tan \frac{\pi}{6}=\tan \frac{7 \pi}{6} \therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}[/math]
'–' চিহ্ন নিয়ে,[math]\begin{array}{l}\tan \theta=-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \Rightarrow \tan \theta=-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}=\tan \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\tan \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\tan \frac{5 \pi}{6}=\tan \frac{11 \pi}{6} \therefore \theta=\frac{5 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi[/math]
 ব্যবধিতে [math]\theta[/math]
 এর মান:[math]\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{2 \pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3}, \frac{11 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #115 (ID: 705750)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: MSB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a \cos ^{2} x+b \sin ^{2} x=c ; a>c>b>0[/math] এবং [math]\sin \theta=\frac{5}{13}[/math]
ক) [math]\sin A+\sin ^{2} A=1[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\cos ^{2} A+\cos ^{4} A=1[/math]
খ) প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\tan x= \pm \sqrt{\frac{c-a}{b-c}}[/math]
গ) [math]\cos \theta[/math] ঋণাত্মক হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]\frac{\tan \theta+\sec (-\theta)^{2}}{\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec}(-\theta)}=\frac{3}{10}[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\sin A+\sin ^{2} A=1[/math]
বা, [math]\sin A=1-\sin ^{2} A[/math]
বা, [math]\sin A=1-\sin ^{2} A[/math]
বা, [math]\sin ^{2} A=\cos ^{4} A[/math]
বা, [math]\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}=\cos ^{4} \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]=[/math]
\therefore \cos ^{2} A+\cos ^{4} A=1$ (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]a \cos ^{2} x+b \sin ^{2} x=c[/math]
বা, [math]a+b \tan ^{2} x=c \sec ^{2} x\left[\cos ^{2} x\right.[/math]
দ্বারা ভাগ করে]বা, [math]a+b \tan ^{2} x=c\left(1+\tan ^{2} x\right)[/math]
বা, [math]a+b \tan ^{2} x=c+c \tan ^{2} x[/math]
বা, [math](b-c) \tan ^{2} x=c-a[/math]
বা, [math]\tan ^{2} x=\frac{c-a}{b-c}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan x= \pm \sqrt{\frac{c-a}{b-c}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{5}{13}[/math]
 এবং [math]\cos \theta[/math]
 ঋণাত্মক হওয়ায় [math]\theta[/math]
 এর অবস্থান দ্বিতীয় চতুর্ভাগে [math]\left(\frac{\pi}{2}<\theta<\pi\right) .[/math]
 [math]\therefore \operatorname{cosec} \theta=\frac{1}{\sin \theta}=\frac{1}{\frac{5}{13}}=\frac{13}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{\pi}{2}<\theta<\pi[/math]
 ব্যবধিতে [math]\tan \theta=-\frac{5}{12}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cot =\frac{-12}{5}[/math]
 এবং [math]\sec \theta=\frac{-13}{12}[/math]

[Image]
বামপক্ষ = [math]=\frac{\tan \theta+\sec (-\theta)}{\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec}(-\theta)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\tan \theta+\sec \theta}{\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-\frac{5}{12}-\frac{13}{12}}{-\frac{12}{5}-\frac{13}{5}}=\frac{-\left(\frac{5}{12}+\frac{13}{12}\right)}{-\left(\frac{12}{5}+\frac{13}{5}\right)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{5+13}{12}}{\frac{12+13}{5}}=\frac{\frac{18}{12}}{\frac{25}{5}}=\frac{18}{12} \times \frac{5}{25}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{90}{300}=\frac{3}{10}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{\tan \theta+\sec (-\theta)}{\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec}(-\theta)}=\frac{3}{10}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:

Question #116 (ID: 705754)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\text { (i) } \operatorname{cosec} \theta=\frac{13}{5}[/math] [math]\text { (ii) }[/math]


[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]45^{\circ} 30^{\prime}[/math] কে রেডিয়ানে প্রকাশ করো।
খ. (i) নং হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{\tan \theta+\sec (-\theta)}{\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec}(-\theta)}=\frac{3}{10}[/math]।
গ. (ii) নং হতে [math]m+\sqrt{n^{2}-m^{2}}=\sqrt{2} n[/math] হলে [math]\alpha[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় করো।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে,প্রদত্ত কোণ [math]=45^{\circ} 30^{\prime}=45^{\circ}+\left(\frac{30}{60}\right)^{\circ}=\left(45+\frac{1}{2}\right)^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{91}{2}^{\circ}=\left(\frac{91 \times 3.1416}{2 \times 180}\right)^{c}=0.7941^{c}[/math]
 (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ
[Image]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta=\frac{13}{5}[/math]
 এবং [math]\frac{\pi}{2}গপ্রদত্ত চিত্রটি,
[Image]
[math]\therefore \frac{m}{n}=\cos \alpha[/math]
 এবং [math]\frac{\sqrt{n^{2}-m^{2}}}{n}=\sin \alpha[/math]
এখানে, [math]m+\sqrt{n^{2}-m^{2}}=\sqrt{2} n[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{m}{n}+\frac{\sqrt{n^{2}-m^{2}}}{n}=\sqrt{2} \\\Rightarrow \cos \alpha+\sin \alpha=\sqrt{2} \\\Rightarrow \cos \alpha=\sqrt{2}-\sin \alpha\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \alpha=2-2 \sqrt{2} \sin \alpha+\sin ^{2} \alpha[/math]
 [বর্গ করে পাই][math]\Rightarrow 1-\sin ^{2} \alpha=2-2 \sqrt{2} \sin \alpha+\sin ^{2} \alpha[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \alpha-2 \sqrt{2} \sin \alpha+1=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (\sqrt{2} \sin \alpha)^{2}-2 \cdot \sqrt{2} \sin \alpha \cdot 1+1^{2}=0 \Rightarrow (\sqrt{2} \sin \alpha-1)^{2}=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sqrt{2} \sin \alpha-1=0 \Rightarrow \sqrt{2} \sin \alpha=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \alpha=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}=\sin \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore \alpha=\frac{\pi}{4} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #117 (ID: 705755)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P=\cot \theta[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{Q}=\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{2 \pi}{9}[/math] রেডিয়ানকে ডিগ্রিতে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. [math]P-Q=m[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\cos \theta=\frac{1-m^{2}}{1+m^{2}}[/math]
গ. [math]P=\frac{12}{5}[/math] এবং [math]\cos \theta[/math] ঋণাত্মক হলে, [math]\frac{\sin \theta+\cos (-\theta)}{\sec (-\theta)+\tan \theta}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\frac{2 \pi}{9}[/math]
 রেডিয়ান [math]=\frac{2}{9} \times 180^{\circ}[/math]
 [ [math]\because \pi[/math]
 রেডিয়ান [math]=180^{\circ}[/math]
 ][math]=40^{\circ} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]P=\cot \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm{Q}=\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]P-Q=m[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta=m\\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}-\frac{1}{\sin \theta}=m\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \theta-1}{\sin \theta}=m \Rightarrow \frac{(\cos \theta-1)^{2}}{\sin ^{2} \theta}=m^{2}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে][math]\Rightarrow \frac{(1-\cos \theta)^{2}}{1-\cos ^{2} \theta}=m^{2} \Rightarrow \frac{(1-\cos \theta)(1-\cos \theta)}{(1+\cos \theta)(1-\cos \theta)}=m^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1-\cos \theta}{1+\cos \theta}=\frac{m^{2}}{1} \Rightarrow \frac{1+\cos \theta}{1-\cos \theta}=\frac{1}{m^{2}}[/math]
 [ব্যস্তকরণ][math]\Rightarrow \frac{1+\cos \theta+1-\cos \theta}{1+\cos \theta-1+\cos \theta}=\frac{1+m^{2}}{1-m^{2}}[/math]
 [যোজন-বিয়োজন][math]\Rightarrow \frac{2}{2 \cos \theta}=\frac{1+m^{2}}{1-m^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos \theta}=\frac{1+m^{2}}{1-m^{2}} \therefore \cos \theta=\frac{1-m^{2}}{1+m^{2}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গসৃজনশীল ২(গ) নং প্রশ্নের সমাধান দ্রষ্টব্য। পৃষ্ঠা-১৪৪

Explanation:

Question #118 (ID: 705756)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{M}=\cos \theta[/math] এবং [math]N=\sin \theta[/math] (যখন [math]0<\theta<2 \pi)[/math])

Options:
ক. [math]\mathrm{B}=\frac{\pi}{3}[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]\sin 2 B=2 \sin B \cos B[/math]
খ. [math]a N-b M=c[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]a M+b N= \pm \sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}[/math]
গ. [math]2 \mathrm{M}^{2}+3 \mathrm{~N}=0[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math] এর সম্ভাব্য মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]B=\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\sin 2 B=\sin \frac{2 \pi}{3}=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)=\sin \frac{\pi}{3}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
ডানপক্ষ [math]=2 \sin B \cdot \cos B=2 \cdot \sin \frac{\pi}{3} \cdot \cos \frac{\pi}{3}=2 \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cdot \frac{1}{2}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin 2 B=2 \sin B \cdot \cos B[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]M=\cos \theta, N=\sin \theta[/math]
এবং [math]a N-b M=c[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow a \sin \theta-b \cos \theta=c\\\Rightarrow (a \sin \theta-b \cos \theta)^{2}=c^{2}\\\Rightarrow a^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta-2 \cdot a \sin \theta \cdot b \cos \theta+b^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta=c^{2}\\\Rightarrow a^{2}\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)-2 \cdot a b \cdot \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta+b^{2}\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)=c^{2}\\\Rightarrow a^{2}-a^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta-2 a \cos \theta \cdot b \sin \theta+b^{2}-b^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta=c^{2}\\\Rightarrow a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}=a^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta+2 a \cos \theta \cdot b \sin \theta+b^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta\\\Rightarrow a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}=(a \cos \theta+b \sin \theta)^{2}\\\Rightarrow a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}=(a M+b N)^{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{aM}+\mathrm{bN}= \pm \sqrt{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}-\mathrm{c}^{2}}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{M}=\cos \theta, \mathrm{N}=\sin \theta[/math]
এবং [math]2 M^{2}+3 N=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore 2 \cos ^{2} \theta+3 \sin \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)+3 \sin \theta=0\\\Rightarrow 2-2 \sin ^{2} \theta+3 \sin \theta=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \theta-3 \sin \theta-2=0[/math]
 [ (-1) দ্বারা গুণ করে ][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \theta-4 \sin \theta+\sin \theta-2=0\\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \theta(\sin \theta-2)+1(\sin \theta-2)=0\\\therefore(\sin \theta-2)(2 \sin \theta+1)=0\end{array}[/math]
হয়, [math]\sin \theta-2=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta=2[/math]
ইহা গ্রহণযোগ্য নয় কারণ, [math]-1 \leq \sin \theta \leq 1[/math]
অথবা, [math]2 \sin \theta+1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \sin \theta=-1\\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=-\frac{1}{2}\\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=-\sin \frac{\pi}{6}\\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\sin \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)\\\therefore \sin \theta=\sin \frac{7 \pi}{6}=\sin \frac{11 \pi}{6}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #119 (ID: 705757)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: SB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin \theta-\cos \theta=p[/math] এবং [math]y \sin A-x \cos A=Q.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]40^{\circ} 35^{\prime} 20^{\prime \prime}[/math] কে রেডিয়ানে প্রকাশ কর ।
খ. [math]P=\frac{7}{13}[/math] হলে, [math](\sin \theta+\cos \theta)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]Q = 0[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math](\sin A-\cos A)^{2}=\frac{(x-y)^{2}}{x^{2}+y^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]40^{\circ} 35^{\prime} 20^{\prime \prime}=40^{\circ}+\left(\frac{35}{60}\right)^{\circ}+\left(\frac{20}{3600}\right)^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\left(40+\frac{7}{12}+\frac{1}{180}\right)^{\circ}=\left(\frac{7200+105+1}{180}\right)^{\circ}=\frac{3653^{\circ}}{90}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{3653}{90} \times \frac{\pi}{180}\right)^{c}[/math]
 [ [math]\because 1^{\circ}=\frac{\pi}{180}[/math]
 রেডিয়ান][math]=\left(\frac{3653 \times 3.1416}{90 \times 180}\right)^{c}=0.7084^{c}[/math]
 (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\sin \theta-\cos \theta=P[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]P=\frac{7}{13}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\text{বা, } \sin \theta-\cos \theta=\frac{7}{13}\\\Rightarrow (\sin \theta-\cos \theta)^{2}=\frac{49}{169}\\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta+\cos ^{2} \theta-2 \sin \theta \cos \theta=\frac{49}{169} \text{.}\\\Rightarrow 1-2 \sin \theta \cos \theta=\frac{49}{169}\\\therefore 2 \sin \theta \cos \theta=1-\frac{49}{169}=\frac{120}{169}\\\therefore(\sin \theta+\cos \theta)^{2}=(\sin \theta-\cos \theta)^{2}+4 \cdot \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{7}{13}\right)^{2}+2 \cdot 2 \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta=\frac{49}{169}+2 \cdot \frac{120}{169}[/math]
 [মান বসিয়ে][math]=\frac{49+240}{169}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (\sin \theta+\cos \theta)^{2}=\frac{289}{169} \Rightarrow \sin \theta+\cos \theta= \pm \sqrt{\frac{289}{169}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta+\cos \theta= \pm \frac{17}{13} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]y \sin A-x \cos A=Q[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]Q=0 \Rightarrow y \sin A-x \cos A=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow y \sin A=x \cos A \Rightarrow \frac{\sin A}{\cos A}=\frac{x}{y} \therefore \tan A=\frac{x}{y}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=(\sin A-\cos A)^{2}=\left\{\cos A\left(\frac{\sin A}{\cos A}-1\right)\right\}^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\cos ^{2} A(\tan A-1)^{2}=\frac{(\tan A-1)^{2}}{\sec ^{2} A} \\=\frac{(\tan A-1)^{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} A}=\frac{\left(\frac{x}{y}-1\right)^{2}}{1+\frac{x^{2}}{y^{2}}}=\frac{\left(\frac{x-y}{y}\right)^{2}}{\frac{y^{2}+x^{2}}{y^{2}}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{(x-y)^{2}}{y^{2}} \times \frac{y^{2}}{x^{2}+y^{2}}=\frac{(x-y)^{2}}{x^{2}+y^{2}}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore(\sin A-\cos A)^{2}=\frac{(x-y)^{2}}{x^{2}+y^{2}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:

Question #120 (ID: 705758)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


চিত্রে [math]\mathrm{OA}=10[/math] সে.মি.

Options:
ক. [math]\theta^{\circ}[/math] কে রেডিয়ানে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. যদি [math]\theta=60^{\circ}[/math] এবং একজন দৌড়বিদ [math]A[/math] বিন্দু থেকে যাত্রা শুরু করে [math]B[/math] বিন্দুতে পৌছাতে 5 সেকেন্ড সময় নেয় তবে তার গতিবেগ নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]2\left(\frac{\mathrm{OM}}{\mathrm{OB}}\right)^{2}=1+2\left(\frac{\mathrm{BM}}{\mathrm{OB}}\right)^{2}[/math] হয় তবে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর। [যেখানে [math]0^{\circ}<\theta<2 \pi[/math]]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কআমরা জানি,[math]180^{\circ}=\pi^{c}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1^{0^{\circ}}=\frac{\pi^{c}}{180}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \theta^{\circ}=\left(\frac{\pi \theta}{180}\right)^{c} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, বৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ, r = OA = 10 সে.মি.কেন্দ্রে উৎপন্ন কোণ, [math]\theta=60^{\circ}[/math]
 সে.মি. :[math]=60 \times \frac{\pi}{180}[/math]
 রেডিয়ান[math]=\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
 রেডিয়ানএখন,চাপ,S [math]S=A B=r \theta[/math]
 [math]=10 \times \frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
 [math]= 10.4719[/math]
 সে.মি.দৌড়বিদ 5 সেকেন্ডে অতিক্রম করে 10.4719 সে.মি.দৌড়বিদ 1 সেকেন্ডে অতিক্রম করে [math]\frac{10.4719}{5}[/math]
 সে.মি.[math]= 2.094[/math]
 সে.মি.[math]\therefore[/math]
 গতিবেগ 2.094 সে.মি./সেকেন্ড [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গউদ্দীপক থেকে পাই,[math]\cos \theta=\frac{\mathrm{OM}}{\mathrm{OB}}[/math]
এবং [math]\sin \theta=\frac{B M}{O B}[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]2\left(\frac{\mathrm{OM}}{\mathrm{OB}}\right)^{2}=1+2\left(\frac{\mathrm{BM}}{\mathrm{OB}}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2} \theta=1+2 \sin ^{2} \theta\\\Rightarrow 2\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)=1+2 \sin ^{2} \theta \text{.}\\\Rightarrow 2-2 \sin ^{2} \theta-1-2 \sin ^{2} \theta=0\\\Rightarrow -4 \sin ^{2} \theta=-1 \text{.}\\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{4}\\\Rightarrow \sin \theta= \pm \frac{1}{2}\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{6}=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \\\therefore \quad \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}\end{array}[/math]
অথবা, [math]\sin \theta=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=-\sin \frac{\pi}{6} \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\sin \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \\\Rightarrow {\theta}=\frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্দিষ্ট সীমার মধ্যে [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #121 (ID: 705759)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: SB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]M=\tan \theta, N=\sec \theta[/math] এবং [math]P=\sin \theta.[/math]

Options:
ক. পৃথিবীর ব্যাসার্ধ 6440 কি.মি। পৃথিবীর উপরের যে দুইটি স্থান কেন্দ্রে [math]7^{\circ}[/math] কোণ উৎপন্ন করে তাদের মধ্যবর্তী দূরত্ব নির্ণয় কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{1-M-N}{N-M-1}=\sqrt{\frac{1+P}{1-P}}.[/math]
গ. [math]P^{2} N-\frac{1}{N}=1[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ; যেখানে [math]0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi.[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কএখানে, পৃথিবীর ব্যাসার্ধ, r = 6440 কি. মি.কোণ [math]\theta=7^{\circ}=\frac{7 \times \pi}{180}[/math]
 রেডিয়ানআমরা জানি, [math]S=r \theta[/math]
 [math]=6440 \times \frac{7 \times \pi}{180}[/math]
 কি. মি.[math]=786.794[/math]
 কি. মি. (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]M=\tan \theta, N=\sec \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]P=\sin \theta[/math]
এখন, বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{1-M-N}{N-M-1}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1-\tan \theta-\sec \theta}{\sec \theta-\tan \theta-1} \\=\frac{\left(\sec ^{2}-\tan ^{2} \theta\right)-\tan \theta-\sec \theta}{\sec \theta-\tan \theta-1} \\=\frac{(\sec \theta+\tan \theta)(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)-(\tan \theta+\sec \theta)}{\sec \theta-\tan \theta-1} \\=\frac{(\sec \theta+\tan \theta)(\sec \theta-\tan \theta-1)}{(\sec \theta-\tan \theta-1)} \\=\sec \theta+\tan \theta \\=\frac{1}{\cos \theta}+\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta} \\=\frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\sqrt{\frac{(1+\sin \theta)^{2}}{\cos ^{2} \theta}} \\=\sqrt{\frac{(1+\sin \theta)^{2}}{1-\sin ^{2} \theta}} \\=\sqrt{\frac{(1+\sin \theta)(1+\sin \theta)}{(1+\sin \theta)(1-\sin \theta)}} \\=\sqrt{\frac{1+\sin \theta}{1-\sin \theta}} \\=\sqrt{\frac{1+P}{1-P}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{1-M-N}{N-M-1}=\sqrt{\frac{1+P}{1-P}}[/math]
 (প্ৰমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\mathrm{P}^{2} \mathrm{~N}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{~N}}=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow (\sin \theta)^{2} \cdot \sec \theta-\frac{1}{\sec \theta}=1 \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin ^{2} \theta}{\cos \theta}-\cos \theta=1 \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin ^{2} \theta-\cos ^{2} \theta}{\cos \theta}=1 \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos ^{2} \theta-\cos ^{2} \theta=\cos \theta \\\Rightarrow 1-2 \cos ^{2} \theta-\cos \theta=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2} \theta+\cos \theta-1=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2} \theta+2 \cos \theta-\cos \theta-1=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \theta(\cos \theta+1)-1(\cos \theta+1)=0 \\\Rightarrow (2 \cos \theta-1)(\cos \theta+1)=0\end{array}[/math]
অর্থাৎ, [math]2 \cos \theta-1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}\\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\cos \frac{\pi}{3}=\cos \frac{5 \pi}{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3}[/math]
অথবা, [math]\cos \theta+1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \theta=-1 \text{.}\\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\cos \pi\\\therefore \theta=\pi\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় মান [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{3}, \pi, \frac{5 \pi}{3} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #122 (ID: 705760)

Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: JB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P=10 \sin ^{2} \alpha+6 \cos ^{2} \alpha[/math] এবং [math]Q=\frac{\sin \theta-\cos \theta+1}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta-1}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{1}{\sin A}=-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}};[/math] যেখানে [math]0<\mathrm{A}<\frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math] হলে [math]A[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]P=7[/math] হলে [math]\cot \alpha[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর। যখন [math]\frac{\pi}{2}<\alpha<\pi.[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{Q}=\frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\sin A=-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
যেখানে, [math]0[math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin A=\sin \left(\frac{5 \pi}{4}\right) \\\therefore \quad A=\frac{5 \pi}{4} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]P=10 \sin ^{2} \alpha+6 \cos ^{2} \alpha[/math]
এবং [math]P=7[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad 10 \sin ^{2} \alpha+6 \cos ^{2} \alpha=7[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 10 \sin ^{2} \alpha+6\left(1-\sin ^{2} \alpha\right)=7\\\Rightarrow 10 \sin ^{2} \alpha+6-6 \sin ^{2} \alpha=7\\\Rightarrow 4 \sin ^{2} \alpha=7-6\\\Rightarrow \cdot \sin ^{2} \alpha=\frac{1}{4} \text{.}\\\Rightarrow \sin \alpha= \pm \frac{1}{2}\\\Rightarrow \sin \alpha=\frac{1}{2}\left[\because \frac{\pi}{2}গদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{aligned}Q & =\frac{\sin \theta-\cos \theta+1}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta-1} \\& =\frac{\cos \theta(\tan \theta-1+\sec \theta)}{\cos \theta(\tan \theta+1-\sec \theta)} \\& =\frac{\tan \theta-1+\sec \theta}{\tan \theta+1-\sec \theta} \\& =\frac{(\tan \theta+\sec \theta)-\left(\sec ^{2} \theta-\tan ^{2} \theta\right)}{1-\sec \theta+\tan \theta}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{(\sec \theta+\tan \theta)-(\sec \theta+\tan \theta)(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)}{1-\sec \theta+\tan \theta} \\=\frac{(\sec \theta+\tan \theta) \cdot(1-\sec \theta+\tan \theta)}{1-\sec \theta+\tan \theta} \\=\sec \theta+\tan \theta \\=\frac{1}{\cos \theta}+\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Question #123 (ID: 705761)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: BB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=15 \cos ^{2} \alpha+2 \sin \alpha, \frac{\pi}{2}<\alpha<\pi[/math] [math]\mathrm{B}=3 \sin ^{2} \theta+5 \cos ^{2} \theta.[/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, রেডিয়ান কোণ একটি ধ্রুব কোণ।
খ. [math]A=7[/math] হলে, [math]\cot \alpha[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]B=4[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপাঠ্যবইয়ের অনুশীলনী- ৮.১ এর প্রতিজ্ঞা- ৪ দ্রষ্টব্য। পৃষ্ঠা- ১৫২ [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]A=7[/math]
 হলে[math]15 \cos ^{2} \alpha+2 \sin \alpha=7[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 15 \cos ^{2} \alpha+2 \sin \alpha-7=0\\\Rightarrow 15-15 \sin ^{2} \alpha+2 \sin \alpha-7=0 \text{.}\\\Rightarrow -15 \sin ^{2} \alpha+2 \sin \alpha+8=0 \text{.}\\\Rightarrow 15 \sin ^{2} \alpha-2 \sin \alpha-8=0\\\Rightarrow 15 \sin ^{2} \alpha-12 \sin \alpha+10 \sin \alpha-8=0\\\Rightarrow 3 \sin \alpha(5 \sin \alpha-4)+2(5 \sin \alpha-4)=0\\\Rightarrow (5 \sin \alpha-4)(3 \sin \alpha+2)=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad 5 \sin \alpha-4=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \alpha=\frac{4}{5}\\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \alpha=\frac{16}{25}\\\Rightarrow 1-\cos ^{2} \alpha=\frac{16}{25}\\\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \alpha=\frac{9}{25}\\\Rightarrow \cos \alpha=-\frac{3}{5}\end{array}[/math]
অথবা, [math]3 \sin \alpha+2=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \alpha=-\frac{2}{3}[/math]
 [math]\frac{\pi}{2}গ [math]B=4[/math]
 হলে, [math]3 \sin ^{2} \theta+5 \cos ^{2} \theta=4[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 3 \sin ^{2} \theta+5-5 \sin ^{2} \theta=4\\\Rightarrow 5-2 \sin ^{2} \theta=4\\\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \theta=1\\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{2}\\\Rightarrow \sin \theta= \pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\text { ' }+ \text { ' }[/math]
 চিহ্ন নিয়ে,[math]\sin \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}=\sin \frac{\pi}{4}=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \theta=\frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]'-'[/math]
 চিহ্ন নিয়ে,[math]\sin \theta=-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}=\sin \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)=\sin \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{5 \pi}{4}, \frac{7 \pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান, [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{3 \pi}{4}, \frac{5 \pi}{4}, \frac{7 \pi}{4} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #124 (ID: 705762)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards:  | Tags: All Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P=\tan \theta+\sec \theta[/math] এবং [math]Q=\cot ^{2} \theta+\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\sec \theta-\tan \theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. দেখাও যে, [math]\cos \theta=\frac{2 P}{P^{2}+1}[/math]
গ. [math]Q=3[/math] হলে, প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটি সমাধান কর, যখন [math]0<\theta<2 \pi \text {. }[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathbf{p}=\tan \theta+\sec \theta[/math]
এখন, [math]\sec ^{2} \theta-\tan ^{2} \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow (\sec \theta+\tan \theta)(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)=1 \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{P}(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)=1 \\\therefore \sec \theta-\tan \theta=\frac{1}{P} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]P=\tan \theta+\sec \theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow P=\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}+\frac{1}{\cos \theta}\\\Rightarrow P=\frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\text { বা, } P^{2}=\frac{(1+\sin \theta)^{2}}{\cos ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{(1+\sin \theta)^{2}}{1-\sin ^{2} \theta}=\mathrm{P}^{2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{(1+\sin \theta)^{2}}{(1+\sin \theta)(1-\sin \theta)}=\mathrm{P}^{2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1+\sin \theta}{1-\sin \theta}=\mathrm{P}^{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1+\sin \theta+1-\sin \theta}{1+\sin \theta-1+\sin \theta}=\frac{\mathrm{P}^{2}+1}{\mathrm{~P}^{2}-1}[/math]
 [যোজন-বিয়োজন করে][math]\Rightarrow \frac{2}{2 \sin \theta}=\frac{P^{2}+1}{P^{2}-1} \Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sin \theta}=\frac{P^{2}+1}{P^{2}-1}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\frac{\mathrm{P}^{2}-1}{\mathrm{P}^{2}+1} \\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta=\frac{\left(\mathrm{P}^{2}-1\right)^{2}}{\left(\mathrm{P}^{2}+1\right)^{2}} \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos ^{2} \theta=\frac{\left(\mathrm{P}^{2}-1\right)^{2}}{\left(\mathrm{P}^{2}+1\right)^{2}} \\\Rightarrow 1-\frac{\left(\mathrm{P}^{2}-1\right)^{2}}{\left(\mathrm{P}^{2}+1\right)^{2}}=\cos ^{2} \theta \\\Rightarrow \frac{\left(\mathrm{P}^{2}+1\right)^{2}-\left(\mathrm{P}^{2}-1\right)^{2}}{\left(\mathrm{P}^{2}+1\right)^{2}}=\cos ^{2} \theta \\\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta=\frac{4 \mathrm{P}^{2}}{\left(\mathrm{P}^{2}+1\right)^{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \theta=\frac{2 P}{\mathrm{P}^{2}+1}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]Q=\cot ^{2} \theta+\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]Q=3[/math]
সুতরাং, [math]\cot ^{2} \theta+\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta=3[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cot ^{2} \theta+1+\cot ^{2} \theta=3\\\Rightarrow 2 \cot ^{2} \theta=2 \text{.}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cot ^{2} \theta=1\\\Rightarrow \cot \theta= \pm 1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\cot \theta=1[/math]
 নিয়ে পাই,[math]\cot\theta=\cot\frac{\pi}{4}=\cot\left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cot \theta=\cot \frac{\pi}{4}=\cot \frac{5 \pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{5 \pi}{4}[/math]
 যা [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]
 শর্ত পূরন করে।আবার, [math]\cot \theta=-1[/math]
 থেকে পাই,[math]\cot \theta=-\cot \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cot \theta=\cot \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{4}\right)=\cot \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{4}\right) \\\Rightarrow \cot \theta=\cot \frac{3 \pi}{4}=\cot \frac{7 \pi}{4}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{3 \pi}{4}, \frac{7 \pi}{4}[/math]
 যা [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]
 শর্ত পূরণ করে।[math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্দিষ্ট সীমার মধ্যে [math]\theta[/math]
 এর সম্ভাব্য মানসমূহ, [math]\frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{3 \pi}{4}, \frac{5 \pi}{4}, \frac{7 \pi}{4} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #125 (ID: 705763)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: DB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=P[/math] এবং [math]Q=\sec \theta-\tan \theta.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]32^{\prime} 4^{\prime \prime}[/math] কে রেডিয়ানে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. [math]P=1[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\sin A-\cos A=\pm 1.[/math]
গ. [math]Q=(\sqrt{3})^{-1}[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর, যেখানে [math]\theta[/math] সূক্ষকোণ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l} 32^{\prime} 4^{\prime \prime}=\left(32 \frac{4}{60}\right)^{\prime}\left[\because 60^{\prime \prime}=1^{\prime}\right] \\ =\left(32 \frac{1}{15}\right)^{\prime}=\left(\frac{481}{15}\right)^{\prime} \\ =\left(\frac{481}{15 \times 60}\right)^{\circ}\left[\because 60^{\prime}=1^{\circ}\right] \\ =\left(\frac{481}{900}\right)^{\circ}=\left(\frac{481}{900} \times \frac{\pi}{180}\right) c\left[\because 1^{\circ}=\frac{\pi^{c}}{180}\right] \\ =\left(\frac{481 \pi}{162000}\right)^{c} \end{array}[/math]
 [math]=.0093^{c}[/math]
 (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\sin \mathrm{A}+\cos \mathrm{A}=\mathrm{P}[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]P=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin A+\cos A=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (\sin A+\cos A)^{2}=1^{2}[/math]
 [উভয়পক্ষকে বর্গ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} A+\cos ^{2} A+2 \sin A \cos A=1\\\Rightarrow 1+2 \sin A \cos A=1 \quad\left[\because \sin ^{2} A+\cos ^{2} A=1\right]\\\Rightarrow 2 \sin A \cos A=1-1\\\therefore 2 \sin A \cos A=0\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math](\sin A-\cos A)^{2}=(\sin A+\cos A)^{2}-4 \sin A \cos A[/math]
 [math]=1^{2}-0[/math]
 [মান বসিয়ে][math]\Rightarrow \sin A-\cos A= \pm \sqrt{1}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin A-\cos A= \pm \sqrt{1}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin A-\cos A= \pm 1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]Q=\sec \theta-\tan \theta[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]Q=(\sqrt{3})^{-1}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sec \theta-\tan \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos \theta}-\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1-\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3}-\sqrt{3} \sin \theta=\cos \theta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{3} \sin \theta)^{2}=(\cos \theta)^{2}[/math]
 [উভয়পক্ষকে বর্গ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 3+3 \sin ^{2} \theta-6 \sin \theta=\cos ^{2} \theta \\\Rightarrow 3+3 \sin ^{2} \theta-6 \sin \theta=1-\sin ^{2} \theta \quad\left[\because \sin ^{2} \theta+\cos ^{2} \theta=1\right] \\\Rightarrow 3 \sin ^{2} \theta+\sin ^{2} \theta-6 \sin \theta+3-1=0 \\\Rightarrow 4 \sin ^{2} \theta-6 \sin \theta+2=0 \\\Rightarrow 2\left(2 \sin ^{2} \theta-3 \sin \theta+1\right)=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \theta-3 \sin \theta+1=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \theta-2 \sin \theta-\sin \theta+1=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \theta(\sin \theta-1)-1(\sin \theta-1)=0 \\\therefore(\sin \theta-1)(2 \sin \theta-1)=0\end{array}[/math]
হয়, [math]\sin \theta-1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=1\\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin 90^{\circ}\\\therefore \theta=90^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
অথবা, [math]2 \sin \theta-1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\frac{1}{2} \text{.}\\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin 30^{\circ}\\\therefore \theta=30^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
কিন্তু [math]\theta=90^{\circ}[/math]
 গ্রহণযোগ্য নয়, কারণ [math]\theta[/math]
 সূক্ষ্মকোণ।[math]\therefore \theta[/math]
 এর মান [math]30^{\circ} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #126 (ID: 705764)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
মুসা ইব্রাহিম দেখল যে, 540 কিলোমিটার দূরে একটি বিন্দুতে কোনো পাহাড় [math]7'[/math] কোণ উৎপন্ন করে এবং তিনি একটি সমীকরণ লিখলেন :

[math]x=\tan \theta+\sec \theta.[/math]

Options:
ক. পাহাড়টির উচ্চতা নির্ণয় কর।
খ. সমীকরণটি হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{x^{2}-1}{x^{2}+1}.[/math]
গ. [math]x=1[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর, যেখানে [math]0^{\circ} \leq \theta<90^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপাঠ্যবইয়ের অনুশীলনী-৮.১ এর উদাহরণ-৯ দ্রষ্টব্য। পৃষ্ঠা-১৫৮ [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\tan \theta+\sec \theta=x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}+\frac{1}{\cos \theta}=x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{(1+\sin \theta)^{2}}{\cos ^{2} \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
 [উভয় পক্ষকে বর্গ করে][math]\Rightarrow \frac{(1+\sin \theta)^{2}}{1-\sin ^{2} \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
 [math]\left[\because \cos ^{2} \theta=1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\frac{(1+\sin \theta)(1+\sin \theta)}{(1+\sin \theta)(1-\sin \theta)}=\mathrm{x}^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\frac{1+\sin \theta}{1-\sin \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1+\sin \theta+1-\sin \theta}{1+\sin \theta-1+\sin \theta}=\frac{\dot{x}^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
 [যোজন-বিয়োজন করে][math]\Rightarrow \frac{2}{2 \sin \theta}=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta=\frac{x^{2}-1}{x^{2}+1}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]x=1[/math]
‘খ’ থেকে পাই, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{x^{2}-1}{x^{2}+1}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\frac{1^{2}-1}{1^{2}+1}[/math]
 [x এর মান বসিয়ে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\frac{0}{2} \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=0 \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin 0^{\circ} \quad\left[\because \sin 0^{\circ}=0\right] \\\therefore \theta=0^{\circ} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #127 (ID: 705765)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: DiB

Question:
একটি গাড়ি ঢাকা থেকে খুলনায় যাওয়ার সময় গাড়ির চাকা প্রতি মিনিটে 720 বার ঘুরে। চাকার ব্যাসার্ধ 0.25 মিটার।

Options:
ক. চাকার পরিধি নির্ণয় কর।
খ. গাড়িটির গতিবেগ নির্ণয় কর।
গ. ঢাকা থেকে খুলনার দূরত্ব পৃথিবীর কেন্দ্রে [math]2^{\circ}[/math] কোণ উৎপন্ন করলে ঢাকা থেকে খুলনায় পৌছাতে গাড়িটির কত সময় লাগবে? [পৃথিবীর ব্যাসার্ধ 6440 কি.মি.]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, চাকার ব্যাসার্ধ, r = 0.25 মিটার[math]\therefore[/math]
 চাকার পরিধি [math]=2 \pi r[/math]
 একক [math]= 2 × 3.1416 × 0.25[/math]
 মিটার[math]= 1.5708[/math]
 মিটার (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ“ক' থেকে পাই, চাকার পরিধি = 1.5708 মিটার (প্রায়)আমরা জানি, চাকা একবার ঘুরে তার পরিধির সমান দূরত্ব অতিক্রম করে।[math]\therefore[/math]
 গাড়িটি প্রতি মিনিটে ঘুরে অতিক্রম করে [math]= 720 × 1.5708[/math]
 মিটার[math]= 1130.976[/math]
 মিটারগাড়িটির গতিবেগ [math]= 1130.976[/math]
 মিটার/মিনিট[math]=\frac{1130.976 \times 60}{1000}[/math]
 কি.মি./ঘন্টা[math]=67.86[/math]
 কি.মি./ঘন্টা [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, ব্যাসার্ধ, R = 6440 কি.মি.পৃথিবীর কেন্দ্রে উৎপন্ন কোণ, [math]\theta=2^{\circ}=2 \times \frac{\pi^{c}}{180}=0.034907^{c}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ঢাকা ও খুলনার মধ্যবর্তী দূরত্ব = চাপের দৈর্ঘ্য [math]=\mathrm{r} \theta[/math]
 [math]=6440 \times 0.034907[/math]
 [math]= 224.801[/math]
 কি.মি.'খ' থেকে পাই, গাড়ীর গতিবেগ [math]= 67.86[/math]
 কি.মি./ঘন্টা[math]\therefore[/math]
 ঢাকা থেকে খুলনায় পৌছাতে সময় লাগবে[math]=(224.801 \div 67.86)[/math]
 ঘন্টা= 3.31 ঘন্টা (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #128 (ID: 705766)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\sec \theta+\tan \theta[/math] এবং [math]B=\cos \left(-\frac{25 \pi}{6}\right)[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]B[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. যদি [math]A=x[/math] হয়, তবে দেখাও যে, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{x^{2}-1}{x^{2}+1}[/math]
গ. [math]\theta[/math] এর সম্ভাব্য মানগুলো নির্ণয় কর যখন [math]A=\sqrt{3}[/math] এবং [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{array}{l}B=\cos \left(-\frac{25 \pi}{6}\right)=\cos \frac{25 \pi}{6}[\because \cos (-\theta)=\cos \theta] \\=\cos \left(4 \pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \\=\cos \left(8 \cdot \frac{\pi}{2}+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\cos \frac{\pi}{6} \\\therefore B=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\sec \theta+\tan \theta[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]A=x[/math]
 [math]\tan \theta+\sec \theta=x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}+\frac{1}{\cos \theta}=x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{(1+\sin \theta)^{2}}{\cos ^{2} \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
 [উভয় পক্ষকে বর্গ করে][math]\Rightarrow \frac{(1+\sin \theta)^{2}}{1-\sin ^{2} \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
 [math]\left[\because \cos ^{2} \theta=1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\frac{(1+\sin \theta)(1+\sin \theta)}{(1+\sin \theta)(1-\sin \theta)}=\mathrm{x}^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\frac{1+\sin \theta}{1-\sin \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1+\sin \theta+1-\sin \theta}{1+\sin \theta-1+\sin \theta}=\frac{\dot{x}^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
 [যোজন-বিয়োজন করে][math]\Rightarrow \frac{2}{2 \sin \theta}=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta=\frac{x^{2}-1}{x^{2}+1}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathbf{A}=\sec \theta+\tan \theta[/math]
শর্তমতে, [math]A=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sec \theta+\tan \theta=\sqrt{3} \\\Rightarrow \sec \theta=\sqrt{3}-\tan \theta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sec ^{2} \theta=(\sqrt{3}-\tan \theta)^{2}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 1+\tan ^{2} \theta=3-2 \sqrt{3} \tan \theta+\tan ^{2} \theta\\\Rightarrow 2 \sqrt{3} \tan \theta=3+\tan ^{2} \theta-1-\tan ^{2} \theta\\\Rightarrow 2 \sqrt{3} \tan \theta=2\\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\frac{2}{2 \sqrt{3}}\\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\tan \frac{\pi}{6}=\tan \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[\because 0<\theta<2 \pi]\\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\tan \frac{\pi}{6}=\tan \frac{7 \pi}{6}\\\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 কিন্তু [math]\theta=\frac{7 \pi}{6}[/math]
 গ্রহণযোগ্য নয়। কারণ [math]\theta=\frac{7 \pi}{6}[/math]
 এর জন্য প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটি সিদ্ধ হয় না ।[math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় মান [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Explanation:
