Question #129 (ID: 705767)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta=m.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]m=2[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\frac{\sin \theta-\cos \theta+1}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta-1}=\frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}.[/math]
গ. [math]m=\sqrt{3}[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর। যেখানে [math]0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi.[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta=m[/math]
আমরা জানি, [math]\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta-\cot ^{2} \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow (\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta)(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)=1 \\\Rightarrow m(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)=1 \\\therefore \operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta=\frac{1}{m} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta=m[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}+\frac{1}{\sin \theta}=2 \quad[\because \mathrm{m}=2][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\frac{\cos \theta+1}{\sin \theta}=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\frac{(\cos \theta+1)^{2}}{\sin ^{2} \theta}=4[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1+\cos \theta}{1-\cos \theta}=4[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1+\cos \theta+1-\cos \theta}{1+\cos \theta-1+\cos \theta}=\frac{4+1}{4-1}[/math]
 [যোজন-বিয়োজন করে][math]\Rightarrow \frac{2}{2 \cos \theta}=\frac{5}{3} \quad \therefore \cos \theta=\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta=\sqrt{1-\cos ^{2} \theta}=\sqrt{1-\left(\frac{3}{5}\right)^{2}}=\sqrt{1-\frac{9}{25}}=\frac{4}{5}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{\sin \theta-\cos \theta+1}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta-1}=\frac{\frac{4}{5}-\frac{3}{5}+1}{\frac{4}{5}+\frac{3}{5}-1}=\frac{\frac{4-3+5}{5}}{\frac{4+3-5}{5}}=\frac{6}{5} \times \frac{5}{2}=3[/math]
ডানপক্ষ [math]=\frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=\frac{1+\frac{4}{5}}{\frac{3}{5}}=\frac{\frac{5+4}{5}}{\frac{3}{5}}=\frac{9}{5} \times \frac{5}{3}=3[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{\sin \theta-\cos \theta+1}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta-1}=\frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,[math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta=m[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta=\sqrt{3} \quad[\because m=\sqrt{3}] \\\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec} \theta=\sqrt{3}-\cot \theta \\\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta=3-2 \sqrt{3} \cot \theta+\cot ^{2} \theta \\\Rightarrow 1+\cot ^{2} \theta-3+2 \sqrt{3} \cot \theta-\cot ^{2} \theta=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \sqrt{3} \cot \theta-2=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cot \theta=\frac{2}{2 \sqrt{3}} \Rightarrow \cot \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \\\Rightarrow \cot \theta=\cot \frac{\pi}{3}=\cot \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)=\cot \frac{4 \pi}{3} \\\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}\end{array}[/math]
কিন্তু [math]\theta=\frac{4 \pi}{3}[/math]
 এর জন্য প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটি সিদ্ধ হয় না।[math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান, [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{3} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #130 (ID: 705768)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: SB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=\sin x[/math]

Options:
ক. 5 সে.মি. ব্যাসার্ধবিশিষ্ট বৃত্তের যে চাপ কেন্দ্রে [math]60^{\circ}[/math] কোণ উৎপন্ন করে তার দৈর্ঘ্য নির্ণয় কর।
খ. যদি [math]a f(\theta)+b f\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\theta\right)=c[/math] হয়, তাহলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]a f\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\theta\right)-b f(\theta)=\pm \sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}.[/math]
গ. সমাধান কর: [math]f(x)+f\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-x\right)=\sqrt{2},[/math] যখন [math]0 \leq x \leq 2 \pi.[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, ব্যাসার্ধ, r = 5 সে.মি.কেন্দ্রে উৎপন্ন কোণ, [math]\theta=60^{\circ}=60 \times \frac{\pi^{c}}{180}=\frac{\pi^{c}}{3}[/math]
আমরা জানি, চাপ [math]S=r \theta=5 \times \frac{\pi}{3}=\frac{5 \times 3.1416}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 চাপের দৈর্ঘ্য [math]= 5.236[/math]
 সে.মি. (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=\sin x[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]a f(\theta)+b f\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\theta\right)=c[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow a \sin \theta+b \sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\theta\right)=c\\\Rightarrow a \sin \theta+b \cos \theta=c\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \quad a^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta+b^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta+2 a b \sin \theta \cos \theta=c^{2}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow a^{2}\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)+b^{2}\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)+2 a b \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta=c^{2}\\\Rightarrow a^{2}-a^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta+b^{2}-b^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta+2 a b \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta=c^{2}\\\Rightarrow a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}=a^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta+b^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta-2 a b \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta\\\Rightarrow a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}=(a \cos \theta)^{2}+(b \sin \theta)^{2}-2 a \cos \theta \cdot b \sin \theta\\\Rightarrow a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}=(a \cos \theta-b \sin \theta)^{2}\\\Rightarrow a \cos \theta-b \sin \theta= \pm \sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad a f\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\theta\right)-b f(\theta)= \pm \sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)+f\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-x\right)=\sqrt{2},[/math]
 যখন [math]0 \leq x \leq 2 \pi[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin x+\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-x\right)=\sqrt{2}\\\Rightarrow \sin x+\cos x=\sqrt{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} x=(\sqrt{2}-\sin x)^{2}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} x=2-2 \sqrt{2} \sin x+\sin ^{2} x\\\Rightarrow 1-\sin ^{2} x=2-2 \sqrt{2} \sin x+\sin ^{2} x\\\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} x-2 \sqrt{2} \sin x+1=0\\\Rightarrow (\sqrt{2} \sin x)^{2}-2 \sqrt{2} \sin x .1+1^{2}=0\\\Rightarrow (\sqrt{2} \sin x-1)^{2}=0\\\Rightarrow \sqrt{2} \sin x-1=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\sin x=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\sin x=\sin \frac{\pi}{4}=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin x=\sin \frac{\pi}{4}=\sin \frac{3 \pi}{4} \quad \therefore x=\frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]
কিন্তু, [math]x=\frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]
 এর জন্য প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটি সিদ্ধ হয় না।[math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান, [math]x=\frac{\pi}{4} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #131 (ID: 705769)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: JB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3 \cos ^{2} \theta=P.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math] হলে, [math]P[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]P=4[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\cot \theta=\pm \sqrt{3}.[/math]
গ. [math]P=6[/math] এবং [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math] এর সম্ভাব্য মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]P=7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3 \cos ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=7\left(\sin \frac{\pi}{4}\right)^{2}+3\left(\cos \frac{\pi}{4}\right)^{2}\left[\because \theta=\frac{\pi}{4}\right] \\=7\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)^{2}+3\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)^{2}=\frac{7}{2}+\frac{3}{2}=\frac{7+3}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore P=5 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খপ্রশ্নমতে, [math]P=4[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3 \cos ^{2} \theta=4 \\\Rightarrow 7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)=4 \\\Rightarrow 7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3-3 \sin ^{2} \theta=4 \\\Rightarrow 4 \sin ^{2} \theta=1 \\\therefore \sin ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{4}\end{array}[/math]
আবার, [math]\cos ^{2} \theta=1-\sin ^{2} \theta=1-\frac{1}{4}=\frac{3}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cot ^{2} \theta=\frac{\cos ^{2} \theta}{\sin ^{2} \theta}=\frac{3}{\frac{1}{4}}=\frac{3}{4} \times \frac{4}{1}=3[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cot \theta= \pm \sqrt{3}[/math]
 (প্ৰমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গপ্রশ্নমতে, [math]P=6[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3 \cos ^{2} \theta=6 \\\Rightarrow 7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)=6 \\\Rightarrow 7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3-3 \sin ^{2} \theta=6 \\\Rightarrow 4 \sin ^{2} \theta=3 \text { বা, } \sin ^{2} \theta=\frac{3}{4} \\\therefore \sin \theta= \pm \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\end{array}[/math]
'+' নিয়ে, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\sin \frac{\pi}{3}=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{2 \pi}{3}[/math]
' [math]-[/math]
' নিয়ে, [math]\sin \theta=-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\sin \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)=\sin \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{4 \pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্দিষ্ট সীমার মধ্যে ৪ এর মানসমূহ:[math]\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{2 \pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #132 (ID: 705770)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: BB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=x \cos \theta[/math] এবং [math]B=\mathrm{y} \sin \theta[/math], যেখানে [math]0<\theta<2 \pi.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{A^{2}}{x^{2}}+\frac{B^{2}}{y^{2}}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]A+B=z[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]x \sin \theta-y \cos \theta=\pm \sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}-z^{2}}.[/math]
গ. [math]x^{2}=3, y^{2}=7[/math] এবং [math]A^{2}+B^{2}=4[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=x \cos \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]B=y \sin \theta[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\frac{A^{2}}{x^{2}}+\frac{B^{2}}{y^{2}}=\frac{(x \cos \theta)^{2}}{x^{2}}+\frac{(y \sin \theta)^{2}}{y^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{x^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta}{x^{2}}+\frac{y^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta}{y^{2}}=\cos ^{2} \theta+\sin ^{2} \theta=1 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A+B=z[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x \cos \theta+y \sin \theta=z[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (x \cos \theta+y \sin \theta)^{2}=z^{2}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow x^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta+y^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta+2 x y \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta=z^{2}\\\Rightarrow x^{2}\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)+y^{2}\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)+2 x y \sin \theta \cos \theta=z^{2}\\\Rightarrow x^{2}-x^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta+y^{2}-y^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta+2 x y \sin \theta \cos \theta=z^{2}\\\Rightarrow x^{2}+y^{2}-z^{2}=x^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta+y^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta-2 x y \sin \theta \cos \theta\\\Rightarrow x^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta+y^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta-2 x y \sin \theta \cos \theta=x^{2}+y^{2}-z^{2}\\\Rightarrow (x \sin \theta-y \cos \theta)^{2}=x^{2}+y^{2}-z^{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore x \sin \theta-y \cos \theta= \pm \sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}-z^{2}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=x \cos \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]B=y \sin \theta[/math]
এখানে, [math]A^{2}+B^{2}=4[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow (x \cos \theta)^{2}+(y \sin \theta)^{2}=4\\\Rightarrow x^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta+y^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta=4\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math]x^{2}=3, y^{2}=7[/math]
 হলে, আমরা পাই, [math]3 \cos ^{2} \theta+7 \sin ^{2} \theta=4[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 3\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)+7 \sin ^{2} \theta=4\\\Rightarrow 3-3 \sin ^{2} \theta+7 \sin ^{2} \theta=4\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3+4 \sin ^{2} \theta=4 \Rightarrow 4 \sin ^{2} \theta=4-3[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 4 \sin ^{2} \theta=1 \Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta= \pm \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [বর্গমূল করে]‘+' নিয়ে, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{6}=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \\\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6} .\end{array}[/math]
'—' নিয়ে, [math]\sin \theta=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=-\sin \frac{\pi}{6} \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\sin \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \frac{7 \pi}{6}=\sin \frac{11 \pi}{6} \\\therefore \theta=\frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #133 (ID: 705745)

Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2024 | Boards:  | Tags: BB

Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. 20° 24' 35" কে রেডিয়ানে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. [math]\frac{y}{x}+\frac{\sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}}}{x}=a[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\cos \theta=\frac{2 a}{a^{2}+1}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\dot{a}}{\mathrm{~b}}+\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\mathrm{a}}=\frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}[/math] হলে [math]θ[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]20^{\circ} 24^{\prime} 35^{\prime \prime}=20^{\circ}+\left(\frac{24}{60}\right)^{\circ}+\left(\frac{35}{60 \times 60}\right)^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\left(20+\frac{2}{5}+\frac{7}{720}\right)^{\circ}=\left(\frac{14400+288+7}{720}\right)^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{14695}{720}\right)^{\circ}=\left(\frac{2939}{144}\right)^{\circ}=\frac{2939}{144} \times \frac{\pi^{\mathrm{c}}}{180}[/math]
 [math]=0.3562^{\mathrm{c}}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ
[Image]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\frac{y}{x}+\frac{\sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}}}{x}=a[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \theta+\sec \theta=\mathrm{a} \cdots \cdots \cdots \text { (i) }[/math]
(i) হতে পাই, [math](\sec \theta+\tan \theta)(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)=a(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)[/math]
বা, [math]\sec ^{2} \theta-\tan ^{2} \theta=a(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)[/math]
বা, [math]1=a(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sec \theta-\tan \theta=\frac{1}{a} \cdots \cdots \cdots \text { (ii) }[/math]
(i) + (ii) করে পাই, [math]2 \sec \theta=\frac{1}{a}+a[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sec \theta=\frac{1+a^{2}}{a}[/math]
বা, [math]\sec \theta=\frac{a^{2}+1}{2 a}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1}{\sec \theta}=\frac{2 a}{a^{2}+1}[/math]
 [ব্যস্তকরণ করে][math]\therefore \cos \theta=\frac{2 a}{a^{2}+1}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{a}=\sin \theta, \mathrm{b}=\cos \theta[/math]
প্রদত্ত সমীকরণ [math]\frac{a}{b}+\frac{b}{a}=\frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}+\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}=\frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \theta+\frac{1}{\tan \theta}=\frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{\tan ^{2} \theta+1}{\tan \theta}=\frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\sqrt{3} \tan ^{2} \theta+\sqrt{3}=4 \tan \theta[/math]
বা, [math]\sqrt{3} \tan ^{2} \theta-4 \tan \theta+\sqrt{3}=0[/math]
বা, [math]\sqrt{3} \tan ^{2} \theta-3 \tan \theta-\tan \theta+\sqrt{3}=0[/math]
বা, [math]\sqrt{3} \tan \theta(\tan \theta-\sqrt{3})-1(\tan \theta-\sqrt{3})=0[/math]
বা, [math](\tan \theta-\sqrt{3})(\sqrt{3} \tan \theta-1)=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \theta-\sqrt{3}=0[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \theta=\sqrt{3}[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \theta=\tan \frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}[/math]
অথবা, [math]\sqrt{3} \tan \theta-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \theta=\tan \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta[/math]
 এর সম্ভাব্য সকল মান [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}, \frac{7 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #134 (ID: 705746)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: DB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\text { (i) } \sin \alpha+\cos \alpha=p[/math] এবং [math]sec \ \alpha+\operatorname{cosec} \alpha=\mathrm{q} \text {}[/math] [math]\text { (ii) } a \cos \theta-b \sin \theta=c[/math]
ক) [math]sin² \ 15° + sin^2 \ 75°[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ) প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]q\left(p^{2}-1\right)=2 p[/math]

Options:
গ. যদি [math]a=b=c= 1[/math] হয়, তবে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর, [math]0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi \text {. }[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
 [math]\sin ^{2} 15^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 75^{\circ}=\sin ^{2} 15^{\circ}+\sin ^{2}\left(90^{\circ}-15^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin ^{2} 15^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 15^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=1\left[\because \sin ^{2} \theta+\cos ^{2} \theta=1\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 খ [math]\\[/math]
উদ্দীপক হতে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin \alpha+\cos \alpha=p \\\sec \alpha+\operatorname{cosec} \alpha=q\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 বামপক্ষ [math]=q\left(p^{2}-1\right)[/math]
 [math]=(\sec \alpha+\operatorname{cosec} \alpha)\left\{(\sin \alpha+\cos \alpha)^{2}-1\right\}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\cos \alpha}+\frac{1}{\sin \alpha}\left(\sin ^{2} \alpha+\cos ^{2} \alpha+2 \sin \alpha \cdot \cos \alpha-1\right)[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{\sin \alpha+\cos \alpha}{\sin \alpha \cos \alpha}\right)(1+2 \sin \alpha \cos \alpha-1)[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{\sin \alpha+\cos \alpha}{\sin \alpha \cos \alpha}\right) \times 2 \sin \alpha \cos \alpha[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=2(\sin \alpha+\cos \alpha) \\=2 \mathrm{p}\end{array}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore q\left(p^{2}-1\right)=2 p[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)গ [math]\\[/math]
উদ্দীপক (ii) হতে পাই,[math]a \cos \theta-b \sin \theta=c[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]a=b=c=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 উদ্দীপকের সমীকরণটি দাঁড়ায়,[math]\text { 1. } \cos \theta-1 . \sin \theta=1[/math]
 যখন [math]0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi[/math]
বা, [math]\cos \theta-\sin \theta=1[/math]
বা, [math]\cos \theta=1^{}+\sin \theta[/math]
বা, [math]\cos ^{2} \theta=1+\sin ^{2} \theta+2 \sin \theta[/math]
 [বর্গ করে]বা, [math]1-\sin ^{2} \theta=1+\sin ^{2} \theta+2 \sin \theta[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sin ^{2} \theta+2 \sin \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore 2 \sin \theta(\sin \theta+1)=0[/math]
হয়, [math]\sin \theta=0[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=\sin 0, \sin 2 \pi[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=0,2 \pi[/math]
অথবা, [math]\sin \theta+1=0[/math]
 [math]\sin \theta=-1[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=\sin \frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math]
 সীমার মধ্যেও এর মানসমূহ [math]=0, \frac{3 \pi}{2}, 2 \pi \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #135 (ID: 705749)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: DiB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]\cos \theta=-\frac{4}{5}, 0<\theta<\pi[/math] হলে, [math]\tan \theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\cot (A+C)=\frac{\cot A \cot C-1}{\cot C+\cot A}+\cot B.[/math]
গ. [math]0 \leq \alpha<2 \pi[/math] সীমার মধ্যে [math]\text { (ii) }[/math] বর্ণিত সমীকরণটি সমাধান কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\cos \theta=-\frac{4}{5}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \quad \sin \theta & =\sqrt{1-\cos ^{2} \theta} \\& =\sqrt{1-\frac{16}{25}} \\& =\frac{3}{5}[\because 0খ
[Image]
এখানে, [math]\angle \mathrm{ACD}=\frac{2 \pi}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \angle A C B=\pi-\frac{2 \pi}{3}=\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
এবং [math]\angle A B C=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \quad \angle {B A C} & =\pi-\left(\frac{\pi}{3}+\frac{\pi}{2}\right) \\& =\frac{\pi}{6}\end{aligned}[/math]
এখন, [math]\cot A=\cot \frac{\pi}{6}=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\cot \mathrm{C}=\cot \frac{\pi}{3}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \\\cot B=\cot \frac{\pi}{2}=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\text{L. H. } S=\cot (A+C)=\cot \left(\frac{\pi}{3}+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\cot \frac{\pi}{2}=0\\\begin{aligned}\text { R. H. } S=\frac{\cot A \cot C-1}{\cot C+\cot A}+\cot B & =\frac{\sqrt{3} \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}-1}{\sqrt{3}+\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}+0 \\& =\frac{1-1}{\sqrt{3}+\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}=0\end{aligned}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \cot (A+C)=\frac{\cot A \cot C-1}{\cot C+\cot A}+\cot B[/math]
 ([প্রমানিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]2 \sin \alpha \cos \alpha+.1=2 \cos \alpha+\sin \alpha[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} 2 \cos \alpha(\sin \alpha-1)=\sin \alpha-1\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \alpha(\sin \alpha-1)-(\sin \alpha-1)=0\\\Rightarrow (\sin \alpha-1)(2 \cos \alpha-1)=0\end{array}[/math]
হয়, [math]\sin \alpha=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \alpha=\sin \frac{\pi}{2} \\\therefore \quad \alpha=\frac{\pi}{2}\end{array}[/math]
অথবা, [math]2 \cos \alpha-1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \alpha=\frac{1}{2}=\cos \frac{\pi}{3}, \cos \frac{5 \pi}{3} \\\therefore \quad \alpha=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান [math]\alpha=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{\pi}{2}, \frac{5 \pi}{3} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #136 (ID: 705720)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2024 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\sin \theta[/math] এবং [math]B=\cos \theta[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\operatorname{cosec} \alpha=\frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{\pi}{2}<\alpha<\pi[/math] হলে, [math]\secα[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\frac{\mathrm{A}}{\mathrm{~B}}=\frac{3}{4}[/math] এবং [math]\sinθ[/math] ঋণাত্মক হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{\cos \theta+\sin \theta}{\sec \theta+\tan \theta}=\frac{14}{5}[/math]
গ. [math]2AB = A[/math] এবং [math]0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi[/math] হলেও [math]θ[/math] এর সম্ভাব্য মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক
[Image]
দেওয়া আছে,[math]\operatorname{cosec} \alpha=\frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sec \alpha=\frac{-\sqrt{5}}{1}\left[\because \frac{\pi}{2}খ
[Image]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\sin \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]B=\cos \theta[/math]
এবং [math]\frac{\mathrm{A}}{\mathrm{~B}}=\frac{3}{4}[/math]
 বা, [math]\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=\frac{3}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \theta=\frac{3}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta=-\frac{3}{5}[\because \sin \theta[/math]
 ঋণাত্মক][math]\therefore \cos \theta=-\frac{4}{5}[\because \tan \theta[/math]
 ধনাত্মক এবং sine ঋণাত্মক তাই ও তৃতীয় চতুর্ভাগে অবস্থিত এবং তৃতীয় চতুর্ভাগে cose ঋণাত্মক][math]\therefore \sec \theta=\frac{1}{\cos \theta}=-\frac{5}{4}[/math]
.: বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{\cos \theta+\sin \theta}{\sec \theta+\tan \theta}=\frac{\frac{-4}{5}+\left(-\frac{3}{5}\right)}{\frac{-5}{4}+\frac{3}{4}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{-4-3}{5}}{\frac{-5+3}{4}}=\frac{\frac{-7}{5}}{\frac{-2}{4}}=\left(-\frac{7}{5}\right) \times\left(\frac{-4}{2}\right)=\frac{14}{5}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{\cos \theta+\sin \theta}{\sec \theta+\tan \theta}=\frac{14}{5}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]2AB = A[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sin \theta \cos \theta=\sin \theta[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sin \theta \cos \theta-\sin \theta=0[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta(2 \cos \theta-1)=0[/math]
হয়, [math]\sin \theta=0[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=\sin 0=\sin \pi=\sin 2 \pi[\because 0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi][/math]
বা, [math]\therefore \theta=0, \pi, 2 \pi[/math]
অথবা, [math]2 \cos \theta-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]\cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}=\cos \frac{\pi}{3}=\cos \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right) {[\because 0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi]}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3}[/math]
.: নির্ধারিত সীমার মধ্যে [math]\theta[/math]
 এর মান [math]=0, \frac{\pi}{3}, \pi, \frac{5 \pi}{3}, 2 \pi \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #137 (ID: 705721)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2024 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB

Question:
[math]\text { (i) } a=\sin \theta, b=\cos \theta[/math]

(ii) ঢাকা ও রাজশাহী পৃথিবীর কেন্দ্রে [math]3°2′3″[/math] কোণ উৎপন্ন করে।

Options:
ক. [math]\sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}+\sin ^{2} \frac{3 \pi}{8}+\sin ^{2} \frac{5 \pi}{8}+\sin ^{2} \frac{7 \pi}{8}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. পৃথিবীর ব্যাসার্ধ 6440 কি.মি. হলে, ঢাকা ও রাজশাহীর মধ্যবর্তী দূরত্ব নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]\frac{\dot{a}}{\mathrm{~b}}+\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\mathrm{a}}=\frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}[/math] হলে, [math]θ[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর, যখন [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}+\sin ^{2} \frac{3 \pi}{8}+\sin ^{2} \frac{5 \pi}{8}+\sin ^{2} \frac{7 \pi}{8}[/math]
 [math]=\sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}+\sin ^{2}\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\pi}{8}\right)+\sin ^{2}\left(\frac{\pi}{2}+\frac{\pi}{8}\right)+\sin ^{2}\left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{8}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}+\cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}+\cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}+\sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}[/math]
 [math]=1+1=2 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,পৃথিবীর ব্যাসার্ধ, r = 6440 কি.মি. ঢাকা ও রাজশাহীর ক্ষেত্রে উৎপন্ন কোণ, [math]\theta=3^{\circ} 2^{\prime} 3^{\prime \prime}[/math]
 [math]=3^{\circ}+\left(\frac{2}{60}\right)^{\circ}+\left(\frac{3}{60 \times 60}\right)^{\circ}=\left(\frac{3641}{1200}\right)^{\circ}=\left(\frac{3641}{1200} \times \frac{\pi}{180}\right)^{c}[/math]
 [math]= 0.053^c[/math]
 (প্রায়).: ঢাকা ও রাজশাহীর মধ্যবর্তী দূরত্ব, [math]S = rθ[/math]
 [math]= (6440 × 0.053)[/math]
 কি.মি.[math]= 341.32[/math]
 কি.মি. (প্রায়) (Ans.)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{a}=\sin \theta, \mathrm{b}=\cos \theta[/math]
প্রদত্ত সমীকরণ [math]\frac{a}{b}+\frac{b}{a}=\frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}+\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}=\frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \theta+\frac{1}{\tan \theta}=\frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{\tan ^{2} \theta+1}{\tan \theta}=\frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\sqrt{3} \tan ^{2} \theta+\sqrt{3}=4 \tan \theta[/math]
বা, [math]\sqrt{3} \tan ^{2} \theta-4 \tan \theta+\sqrt{3}=0[/math]
বা, [math]\sqrt{3} \tan ^{2} \theta-3 \tan \theta-\tan \theta+\sqrt{3}=0[/math]
বা, [math]\sqrt{3} \tan \theta(\tan \theta-\sqrt{3})-1(\tan \theta-\sqrt{3})=0[/math]
বা, [math](\tan \theta-\sqrt{3})(\sqrt{3} \tan \theta-1)=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \theta-\sqrt{3}=0[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \theta=\sqrt{3}[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \theta=\tan \frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}[/math]
অথবা, [math]\sqrt{3} \tan \theta-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \theta=\tan \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]θ[/math]
 এর সম্ভাব্য সকল মান, [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}, \frac{7 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #138 (ID: 705722)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2024 | Boards:  | Tags: SB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sec \theta-\tan \theta=P[/math] এবং [math]2 \cos ^{2} \theta+2 \sqrt{2} \sin \theta=\mathrm{Q}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]15'7"[/math] কে রেডিয়ানে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. [math]P = x[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta=\frac{1+x^{2}}{1-x^{2}}[/math]
গ. [math]Q = 3[/math] এবং [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math] হলে, [math]θ[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত কোণ [math]= 15'7"[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{15}{60}\right)^{\circ}+\left(\frac{7}{60 \times 60}\right)^{\circ}=\frac{1^{\circ}}{4}+\frac{7^{\circ}}{3600}=\frac{907^{\circ}}{3600}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{907}{3600} \times \frac{\pi}{180}\right)^{\circ}[/math]
 রেডিয়ান[math]= 0.0044[/math]
 রেডিয়ান (প্রায়) (Ans.)[math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, P = xবা, [math]\sec \theta-\tan \theta=x[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1}{\cos \theta}-\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=x[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1-\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=x[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{(1-\sin \theta)^{2}}{\cos ^{2} \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে]বা, [math]\frac{(1-\sin \theta)^{2}}{(1+\sin \theta)(1-\sin \theta)}=x^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1-\sin \theta}{1+\sin \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1+\sin \theta}{1-\sin \theta}=\frac{1}{x^{2}}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1+\sin \theta+1-\sin \theta}{1+\sin \theta-1+\sin \theta}=\frac{1+x^{2}}{1-x^{2}}[/math]
 [যোজন-বিয়োজন করে]বা, [math]\frac{2}{2 \sin \theta}=\frac{1+x^{2}}{1-x^{2}}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1}{\sin \theta}=\frac{1+x^{2}}{1-x^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \operatorname{cosec} \theta=\frac{1+\mathrm{x}^{2}}{1-\mathrm{x}^{2}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]Q = 3[/math]
বা, [math]2 \cos ^{2} \theta+2 \sqrt{2} \sin \theta=3[/math]
বা, [math]2-2 \sin ^{2} \theta+2 \sqrt{2} \sin \theta=3[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sin ^{2} \theta-2 \sqrt{2} \sin \theta+1=0[/math]
বা, [math](\sqrt{2} \sin \theta)^{2}-2 \sqrt{2} \sin \theta \cdot 1+1^{2}=0[/math]
বা, [math](\sqrt{2} \sin \theta-1)^{2}=0[/math]
বা, [math]\sqrt{2} \sin \theta=1[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{4}=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{4}=\sin \frac{3 \pi}{4} \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]
 হলে, [math]θ[/math]
 এর মান [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{3 \pi}{4} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #139 (ID: 705723)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2024 | Boards:  | Tags: JB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=x \cos \theta, B=y \sin \theta[/math]

Options:
ক. সকাল 8:30 টায় ঘড়ির ঘণ্টার কাঁটা ও মিনিটের কাঁটার অন্তর্গত কোণকে ডিগ্রিতে নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]A + B = z[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]x \sin \theta-y \sin \theta= \pm \sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}-z^{2}}[/math]
গ. [math]x ^ 2 = 3 , y ^ 2 = 7[/math] এবং [math]A ^ 2 + B ^ 2 = 4[/math] হলে, [math]θ[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর। (যখন [math]0<\theta<2 \pi)[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কআমরা জানি,ঘড়িতে সর্বমোট 12টি ঘন্টার দাগ কাঁটা থাকে।.: ঘন্টার কাঁটার ক্ষেত্রে 12 ঘন্টা কেন্দ্রে উৎপন্ন করে = 360°.: ঘন্টার কাঁটার ক্ষেত্রে 1 ঘন্টা কেন্দ্রে উৎপন্ন করে [math]=\frac{360^{\circ}}{12}=30^{\circ}[/math]
.: ঘন্টার কাঁটার ক্ষেত্রে 1 মিনিট কেন্দ্রে উৎপন্ন করে [math]=\frac{30^{\circ}}{60}=0.5^{\circ}[/math]
 [ 1 ঘন্টা = 60 মি.].: ঘন্টার কাঁটার ক্ষেত্রে 30 মিনিট কেন্দ্রে উৎপন্ন করে [math]= 0.5 × 30 = 15°[/math]
.: সকাল 8:30 টায় ঘড়ির ঘন্টার কাঁটা ও মিনিটের কাঁটার অন্তর্গত কোণ [math]= 2 × 30° +15° =60° +15°= 75°[/math]
 (Ans.)[math]\\[/math]
 খবিশেষ দ্রষ্টব্য: প্রশ্নটি ত্রুটিপূর্ণ। [math]x \cos \theta+y \sin \theta=z[/math]
 হলে,[math]\mathrm{x} \sin \theta-\mathrm{y} \sin \theta= \pm \sqrt{\mathrm{x}^{2}+\mathrm{y}^{2}-\mathrm{z}^{2}}[/math]
 প্রমাণ করা অসম্ভব।তাই [math]x \sin \theta-y \sin \theta[/math]
 পরিবর্তে [math]x \sin \theta-y \cos \theta[/math]
 বিবেচনা করে সমাধান দেওয়া হলো।দেওয়া আছে, [math]A=xcosθ[/math]
 ও [math]B = ysinθ[/math]
এবং [math]A + B = z[/math]
 বা , [math]xcosθ + ysinθ = z[/math]
বা, [math](x \cos \theta+y \sin \theta)^{2}=z^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]x^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta+2 \cdot x \cos \theta \cdot y \sin \theta+y^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta=z^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]x^{2}\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)+2 x y \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta+y^{2}\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)=z^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]x^{2}-x^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta+2 x y \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta+y^{2}-y^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta=z^{2}[/math]
বা, [math](x \sin \theta-y \cos \theta)^{2}=x^{2}+y^{2}-z^{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{x} \sin \theta-\mathrm{y} \cos \theta= \pm \sqrt{\mathrm{x}^{2}+\mathrm{y}^{2}-\mathrm{z}^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]A = x cosθ, B = y sinθ[/math]
 এবং [math]x ^ 2 = 3 y²[/math]
এখানে, [math]A ^ 2 + B ^ 2 = 4[/math]
বা, [math]x^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta+y^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta=4[/math]
বা, [math]7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3 \cos ^{2} \theta=4[/math]
বা, [math]7 \sin ^{2} \theta+3-3 \sin ^{2} \theta=4[/math]
বা, [math]4 \sin ^{2} \theta=1[/math]
বা, [math]\sin ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{4}[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta= \pm \frac{1}{2}[/math]
এখন, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 হলে [math]\sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{6}=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\sin \frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
আবার , [math]\sin \theta=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 হলে[math]\sin \theta=-\sin \frac{\pi}{6}=\sin \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\sin \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]\sin \theta=\sin \frac{7 \pi}{6}=\sin \frac{11 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]
 ব্যবধিতে নির্ণেয় মান, [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #140 (ID: 705733)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P=\cot \theta, Q=\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{R}=\cos \theta.[/math]

Options:
ক. চিত্রসহ [math]-510^{\circ}[/math] কোণের অবস্থান কোন চতুর্ভাগে নির্ণয় কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{1-P-Q}{Q-P-1}=\sqrt{\frac{1+R}{1-R}}[/math]
গ. [math]\mathrm{R}^{2} \cdot \mathrm{Q}-\frac{1}{Q}=1[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় করো। যেখানে, [math]0 \leq \theta \leq \pi[/math]।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক
[Image]
কোণের মান [math]-510^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=-450^{\circ}-60^{\circ} \\=-5 \times 90^{\circ}-60^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
অর্থাৎ, [math]-510^{\circ}[/math]
 কোণটি তৃতীয় চতুর্ভাগে অবস্থিত। [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]P=\cot \theta, Q=\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm{R}=\cos \theta[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{1-P-Q}{Q-P-1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta}{\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta-1}[/math]
 [P ও Q এর মান বসিয়ে][math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1-\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta}{(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)-\left(\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta-\cot ^{2} \theta\right)} \\=\frac{1-\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta}{(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)-(\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta)(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)} \\=\frac{1-\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta}{(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)(1-\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)} \\=\frac{1}{\frac{1}{\sin \theta}-\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}}=\frac{1}{\frac{1-\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}}=\frac{\sin \theta}{1-\cos \theta}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\sqrt{\frac{\sin ^{2} \theta}{(1-\cos \theta)^{2}}} \\=\sqrt{\frac{1-\cos ^{2} \theta}{(1-\cos \theta)^{2}}} \\=\sqrt{\frac{(1+\cos \theta)(1-\cos \theta)}{(1-\cos \theta)(1-\cos \theta)}} \\=\sqrt{\frac{1+\cos \theta}{1-\cos \theta}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{1+R}{1-R}}[/math]
 [R এর মান বসিয়ে][math]=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{1-P-Q}{Q-P-1}=\sqrt{\frac{1+R}{1-R}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]R^{2} \cdot Q-\frac{1}{Q}=1 ; 0 \leq \theta \leq \pi[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta \cdot \operatorname{cosec} \theta-\frac{1}{\operatorname{cosec} \theta}=1[/math]
 [Q ও R এর মান বসিয়ে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1-\sin ^{2} \theta}{\sin \theta}-\sin \theta=1 \\\Rightarrow \frac{1-\sin ^{2} \theta-\sin ^{2} \theta}{\sin \theta}=1 \\\Rightarrow 1-2 \sin ^{2} \theta=\sin \theta \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \theta+\sin \theta-1=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \theta+2 \sin \theta-\sin \theta-1=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \theta(\sin \theta+1)-1(\sin \theta+1)=0 \\\Rightarrow (2 \sin \theta-1)(\sin \theta+1)=0\end{array}[/math]
হয়, [math]2 \sin \theta-1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\frac{1}{2} \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{6}=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{6}=\sin \frac{5 \pi}{6} \\\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}\end{array}[/math]
অথবা, [math]\sin \theta+1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=-1 \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=-\sin \frac{\pi}{2} \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{2}\right)=\sin \frac{3 \pi}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [গ্রহণযোগ্য নয় যেহেতু [math]0 \leq \theta \leq \pi[/math]
 ][math]\therefore 0 \leq \theta \leq \pi[/math]
 ব্যবধিতে [math]\theta[/math]
 এর মান [math]=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #141 (ID: 705734)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: DB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{\tan \theta=a, \sec \theta=b}[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{\frac{\cos \theta}{1-\sin \theta}=c}[/math]

Options:
ক. ত্রিভুজের তিনটি কোণের অনুপাত [math]5: 6: 7[/math] হলে ক্ষুদ্রতম কোণটিকে রেডিয়ানে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{\frac{a+b-1}{a-b+1}=c}[/math]
গ. [math]\mathrm{c=\sqrt{3}}[/math] হলে [math]\mathrm{\theta}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর, যখন [math]\mathrm{0<\theta \leq 2 \pi}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কমনে করি, কোণ তিনটি 5x, 6x ও 7x রেডিয়ান।আমরা জানি, ত্রিভুজের তিন কোণের সমষ্টি 180° বা [math]\pi[/math]
 রেডিয়ান।[math]\therefore \quad 5 x+6 x+7 x=\pi[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 18 x=\pi[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad x=\frac{\pi}{18}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ক্ষুদ্রতম কোণ [math]=5 x=5 \times \frac{\pi}{18}[/math]
 রেডিয়ান[math]=\frac{5 \pi}{18}[/math]
 রেডিয়ান [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{array}{c}\tan \theta=a \\\sec \theta=b\end{array}[/math]
এবং [math]\frac{\cos \theta}{1-\sin \theta}=c[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{a+b-1}{a-b+1}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\tan \theta+\sec \theta-1}{\tan \theta-\sec \theta+1} \\=\frac{\sec \theta+\tan \theta-1}{\sec ^{2} \theta-\tan ^{2} \theta+\tan \theta-\sec \theta} \\=\frac{\sec \theta+\tan \theta-1}{(\sec \theta+\tan \theta)(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)-(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)} \\=\frac{(\sec \theta+\tan \theta-1)}{(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)(\sec \theta+\tan \theta-1)} \\=\frac{1}{\sec \theta-\tan \theta} \\=\frac{1}{\frac{1}{\cos \theta}-\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\cos \theta}{1-\sin \theta} \\=c\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{a+b-1}{a-b+1}=c[/math]
 (প্ৰমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]c=\frac{\cos \theta}{1-\sin \theta}[/math]
আবার, [math]c=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \frac{\cos \theta}{1-\sin \theta}=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos ^{2} \theta}{(1-\sin \theta)^{2}}=3[/math]
 [বর্গ করে][math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta=3(1-\sin \theta)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 1-\sin ^{2} \theta=3\left(1-2 \sin \theta+\sin ^{2} \theta\right) \\\Rightarrow 1-\sin ^{2} \theta=3-6 \sin \theta+3 \sin ^{2} \theta \\\Rightarrow 4 \sin ^{2} \theta-6 \sin \theta+2=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \theta-3 \sin \theta+1=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \theta-2 \sin \theta-\sin \theta+1=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \theta(\sin \theta-1)-1(\sin \theta-1)=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad(\sin \theta-1)(2 \sin \theta-1)=0[/math]
হয়, [math]\sin \theta-1=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \theta=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
অথবা, [math]2 \sin \theta-1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \quad \sin \theta=\frac{1}{2}\\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{6}=\sin \frac{5 \pi}{6}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 এবং [math]\frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
 এর জন্য [math]c=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 সিদ্ধ নয়।[math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান, [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #142 (ID: 705735)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x=a \cos \theta[/math] এবং [math]y=b \sin \theta.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{x}{y}=1[/math] হলে [math]\frac{a \sin \theta+b \cos \theta}{a \sin \theta-b \cos \theta}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]x-y=\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]a \sin \theta+b \cos \theta-c=0.[/math]
গ. [math]a=3[/math] এবং [math]b=\sqrt{2}[/math] হলে [math]x+y^{2}=3[/math] সমীকরণটি সমাধান কর, যখন [math]0 \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi.[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{array}{l}x=a \cos \theta \\y=b \sin \theta\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math]\frac{x}{y}=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\mathrm{a} \cos \theta}{\mathrm{b} \sin \theta}=1 \\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\frac{\mathrm{b} \sin \theta}{\mathrm{a}}\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math]\frac{a \sin \theta+b \cos \theta}{a \sin \theta-b \cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{a \sin \theta+b \cdot \frac{b \sin \theta}{a}}{a \sin \theta-b \cdot \frac{b \sin \theta}{a}} \\=\frac{\frac{\sin \theta}{a}\left(a^{2}+b^{2}\right)}{\frac{\sin \theta}{a}\left(a^{2}-b^{2}\right)} \\=\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}}{a^{2}-b^{2}} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]x-y=\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow a \cos \theta-b \sin \theta=\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}\\\Rightarrow (a \cos \theta-b \sin \theta)^{2}=a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}\\\Rightarrow a^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta-2 a b \cdot \cos \theta \cdot \sin \theta+b^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta=a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow a^{2}\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)-2 a b \cdot \cos \theta \cdot \sin \theta+\dot{b}^{2}\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)=a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}\\\Rightarrow a^{2}+b^{2}-a^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta-2 a b \cos \theta \cdot \sin \theta-b^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta\\\Rightarrow -\left(a^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta+2 a \sin \theta \cdot b \cos \theta+b^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta\right)=a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}\\\Rightarrow \left.(a \sin \theta+b \cos \theta)^{2}=c^{2} \cos \theta+b^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta\right)=-c^{2}\\\Rightarrow a \sin \theta+b \cos \theta=c\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad a \sin \theta+b \cdot \cos \theta-c=0[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]x=a \cos \theta, y=b \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]a=3[/math]
 এবং [math]b=\sqrt{2}[/math]
 হলে,[math]y=\sqrt{2} \sin \theta[/math]
এখন, [math]x+y^{2}=3[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 3 \cos \theta+(\sqrt{2} \sin \theta)^{2}=3 \text{.}\\\Rightarrow 3 \cos \theta+2\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)=3\\\Rightarrow 3 \cos \theta+2-2 \cos ^{2} \theta-3=0\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2} \theta-3 \cos \theta+1=0\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2} \theta-2 \cos \theta-\cos \theta+1=0\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \theta(\cos \theta-1)-1(\cos \theta-1)=0\\\Rightarrow (\cos \theta-1)(2 \cos \theta-1)=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \cos \theta-1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \theta=1 \\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\cos \theta=\cos 2 \pi \\\therefore \quad \theta=0,2 \pi\end{array}[/math]
অথবা, [math]2 \cos \theta-1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}\\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\cos \frac{\pi}{3} \\=\cos \frac{5 \pi}{3} \\\therefore \quad \theta=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3} \\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধানঃ [math]\theta=0, \frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3}, 2 \pi \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #143 (ID: 705736)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]X=\frac{\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A-1}{\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A+1}[/math] এবং [math]Y=\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]A=\frac{2 \pi}{3}[/math] হলে [math]Y[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]XY=-1[/math]
গ. [math]Y=(\sqrt{3})^{-1}[/math] এবং [math]0 \leq \mathrm{A} \leq 2 \pi[/math] হলে [math]A[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]A=\frac{2 \pi}{3}[/math]
 হলে,[math]\begin{aligned}Y & =\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A \\& =\cot \frac{2 \pi}{3}-\operatorname{cosec} \frac{2 \pi}{3} \\& =\cot 120^{\circ}-\operatorname{cosec} 120^{\circ} \\& =\cot \left(90^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)-\operatorname{cosec}\left(90^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right) \\& =-\tan 30^{\circ}-\sec 30^{\circ} \\& =-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}-\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{-1-2}{\sqrt{3}} \\=\frac{-3}{\sqrt{3}} \\=-\sqrt{3} \text { (Ass.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\begin{aligned}X & =\frac{\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A-1}{\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A+1} \\& =\frac{\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A-\left(\operatorname{cosec}{ }^{2} A-\cot ^{2} A\right)}{\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A+1} \\& =\frac{\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A-(\operatorname{cosec} A+\cot A)\left(\operatorname{cosec} A-\cot A\right)}{\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A+1} \\& =\frac{(\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A)(1-\operatorname{cosec} A+\cot A)}{(1-\operatorname{cosec} A+\cot A)} \\& =\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A \\& X Y=(\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A)(\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A) \\& =\cot ^{2} A-\operatorname{cosec} A \\& =-\left(\operatorname{cosec} A-\cot ^{2} A\right)\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]=-1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,[math]Y=(\sqrt{3})^{-1}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos A}{\sin A}-\frac{1}{\sin A}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos A-1}{\sin A}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{(\cos \mathrm{A}-1)^{2}}{\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}=\frac{1}{3}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{(\cos A-1)^{2}}{\left(1-\cos ^{2} A\right)}=\frac{1}{3} \text{.}\\\Rightarrow \frac{(1-\cos A)^{2}}{(1-\cos A)(1+\cos A)}=\frac{1}{3}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1-\cos A}{1+\cos A}=\frac{1}{3}\\\Rightarrow 3-3 \cos A=1+\cos A\\\Rightarrow 3-1=\cos A+3 \cos A\\\Rightarrow 4 \cos A=2\\\Rightarrow \cos A=\frac{1}{2}=\cos \frac{\pi}{3}, \cos \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad A=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3}[/math]
কিন্তু [math]A=\frac{\pi}{3}, \cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A=(\sqrt{3})^{-1}[/math]
 সমীকরণটিকে সিদ্ধ করে না।[math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় মান [math]A=\frac{5 \pi}{3} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #144 (ID: 705707)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2024 | Boards:  | Tags: MSB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P=\frac{\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A-1}{\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A+1}[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{R}=\tan \alpha+\sec \alpha[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]-315^{\circ}[/math] কোণটি কোন চতুর্ভাগে অবস্থিত চিত্রসহ নির্ণয় কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]P=\sqrt{\frac{\sec A+1}{\sec A-1}}[/math]
গ. যদি [math]\mathrm{R}=\sqrt{3}[/math] এবং [math]0<α<2 π[/math] হয়, তবে [math]α[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক
[Image]
[math]-315°=-3 \times 90°-45°[/math]
.:. [math]- 315°[/math]
 কোণটি প্রথম চতুর্ভাগে অবস্থিত। [math](Ans.)[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]P=\frac{\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A-1}{\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A+1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A-\left(\operatorname{cosec}^{2} A-\cot ^{2} A\right)}{\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A+1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A+(\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A)(\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A)}{\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A+1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{(\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A)(\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A+1)}{(\cot A-\operatorname{cosec} A+1)}[/math]
 [math]=\cot A+\operatorname{cosec} A[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos A}{\sin A}+\frac{1}{\sin A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1+\cos A}{\sin A}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{(1+\cos A)^{2}}{\sin ^{2} A}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{(1+\cos A)^{2}}{1-\cos ^{2} A}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{(1+\cos A)^{2}}{(1+\cos \mathrm{A})(1-\cos \mathrm{A})}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{1+\cos \mathrm{A}}{1-\cos \mathrm{A}}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{1+\frac{1}{\sec \mathrm{~A}}}{1-\frac{1}{\sec \mathrm{~A}}}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{\frac{\sec \mathrm{A}+1}{\sec \mathrm{~A}}}{\frac{\sec \mathrm{~A}-1}{\sec \mathrm{~A}}}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{\sec \mathrm{A}+1}{\sec \mathrm{~A}-1}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore P=\sqrt{\frac{\sec A+1}{\sec A-1}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{R}=\tan \alpha+\sec \alpha[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{R}=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 হলে,[math]\therefore \tan \alpha+\sec \alpha=\sqrt{3}[/math]
বা, [math]\sec \alpha =\sqrt{3}=\tan \alpha[/math]
বা, [math]\sec ^{2} \alpha=(\sqrt{3}-\tan \alpha)^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]1+\tan ^{2} \alpha=3-2 \sqrt{3} \tan \alpha+\tan ^{2} \alpha[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sqrt{3} \tan \alpha=2[/math]
বা, [math]\tan \alpha=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \tan \frac{\pi}{6} \tan \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[\because 0 < \alpha <2 \pi][/math]
বা, [math]\tan \alpha=\tan \frac{\pi}{6} \tan \frac{7 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \alpha=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\alpha=\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 হলে [math]\tan \frac{\pi}{6}+\sec \frac{\pi}{6}-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}+\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}=\frac{3}{\sqrt{3}}=\sqrt{3}[/math]
এবং [math]\alpha=\frac{7 \pi}{6}[/math]
 হলে[math]\tan \frac{7 \pi}{6}+\sec \frac{7 \pi}{6}=\tan \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)+\sec \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)^{2} \tan \frac{\pi}{6}-\sec \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}-\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}=-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \alpha=\frac{7 \pi}{6}[/math]
 এর জন্য প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটি সিদ্ধ হয় না।[math]\therefore \alpha=\frac{\pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #145 (ID: 705708)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2024 | Boards:  | Tags: RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a = \cot \theta[/math] এবং [math]b = cosec \ θ[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]4θ = π[/math] হলে, [math]a + b ^ 2[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]a + b = x[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]\sec \theta=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
গ. [math]3(a ^ 2 + b ^ 2) = 5[/math] এবং [math]0 < θ < 2π[/math] হলে [math]θ[/math] এর সম্ভাব্য মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]4 \theta=\pi \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
আবার, [math]a = cotθ[/math]
 এবং [math]b = cosecθ[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=a+b^{2}=\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]=\cot \frac{\pi}{4}+\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \frac{\pi}{4}=1+(\sqrt{2})^{2}=1+2=3 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]a = cotθ[/math]
 এবং [math]b = cosecθ[/math]
প্রদত্ত সমীকরণ, [math]a + b = x[/math]
বা, [math]\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta=x[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1}{\sin \theta}+\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}=x[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1+\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}=x[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{(1+\cos \theta)^{2}}{\sin ^{2} \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে]বা, [math]\frac{(1+\cos \theta)^{2}}{1-\cos ^{2} \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{(1+\cos \theta)(1+\cos \theta)}{(1+\cos \theta)(1-\cos \theta)}=x^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1+\cos \theta}{1-\cos \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1+\cos \theta+1-\cos \theta}{1+\cos \theta-1+\cos \theta}=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
 [যোজন-বিয়োজন করে]বা, [math]\frac{2}{2 \cos \theta}=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1}{\cos \theta}=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sec \theta=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]a = cotθ[/math]
 এবং [math]b = cosecθ[/math]
প্রদত্ত সমীকরণ, [math]3(a ^ 2 + b ^ 2) = 5[/math]
বা, [math]3 \cot ^{2} \theta+3 \operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta=5[/math]
বা, [math]\cot ^{2} \theta+\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta=\frac{5}{3}[/math]
বা, [math]\cot ^{2} \theta+1+\cot ^{2} \theta=\frac{5}{3}[/math]
বা, [math]2 \cot ^{2} \theta=\frac{5}{3}-1=\frac{2}{3}[/math]
বা, [math]\cot ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{3}[/math]
বা, [math]\cot \theta= \pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
এখন, [math]\cot \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 থেকে পাই, [math]\cot \theta=\cot \frac{\pi}{3}=\cot \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}[\because 0<\theta<2 \pi][/math]
আবার, [math]\cot \theta=\frac{-1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 থেকে পাই, [math]\cot \theta=\cot \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)=\cot \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{2 \pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3}[\because 0<\theta<2 \pi][/math]
.: নির্দিষ্ট সীমা [math]0 < θ < 2π[/math]
 এর মধ্যে [math]θ[/math]
 এর সম্ভাব্যমানসমূহ, [math]\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{2 \pi}{3}, \frac{4 \pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{3} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #146 (ID: 705709)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2024 | Boards:  | Tags: DiB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a = cosecθ[/math] এবং [math]b = cot θ[/math] [math]\\[/math]

Options:
ক. একটি ত্রিভুজের তিনটি কোণের অনুপাত [math]3:5:7[/math] হলে, বৃহত্তম কোণের বৃত্তীয়মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]a + b = x[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]\sec \theta=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
গ. [math]3a ^ 2 + 2b ^ 2 = 18[/math] এবং [math]0 < \theta < 2\pi[/math] হলে, ও এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কধরি, ত্রিভুজের কোণত্রয় [math]3x, 5x[/math]
 ও [math]7x[/math]
শর্তমতে, [math]3x + 5x + 7x = \pi ^ c[/math]
বা, [math]15 x=\pi^{c}[/math]
 [math]\therefore x=\frac{\pi^{c}}{15}[/math]
∴ বৃহত্তম কোণ [math]=7 \mathrm{x}=\frac{7 \pi^{\mathrm{c}}}{15} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]a = cotθ[/math]
 এবং [math]b = cosecθ[/math]
প্রদত্ত সমীকরণ, [math]a + b = x[/math]
বা, [math]\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta=x[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1}{\sin \theta}+\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}=x[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1+\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}=x[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{(1+\cos \theta)^{2}}{\sin ^{2} \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে]বা, [math]\frac{(1+\cos \theta)^{2}}{1-\cos ^{2} \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{(1+\cos \theta)(1+\cos \theta)}{(1+\cos \theta)(1-\cos \theta)}=x^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1+\cos \theta}{1-\cos \theta}=x^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1+\cos \theta+1-\cos \theta}{1+\cos \theta-1+\cos \theta}=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
 [যোজন-বিয়োজন করে]বা, [math]\frac{2}{2 \cos \theta}=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1}{\cos \theta}=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sec \theta=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]a = cosecθ[/math]
 এবং [math]b = cot θ[/math]
প্রদত্ত সমীকরণ,বা, [math]3 a^{2}+2 b^{2}=18[/math]
বা, [math]3 \operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta+2 \cot ^{2} \theta=18[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{3}{\sin ^{2} \theta}+\frac{2 \cos ^{2} \theta}{\sin ^{2} \theta}=18[/math]
বা, [math]3+2 \cos ^{2} \theta=18 \sin ^{2} \theta[/math]
বা, [math]3+2\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)=18 \sin ^{2} \theta[/math]
বা, [math]3+2-2 \sin ^{2} \theta=18 \sin ^{2} \theta[/math]
বা, [math]20 \sin ^{2} \theta=5[/math]
বা, [math]\sin ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta= \pm \frac{1}{2}[/math]
হয়, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
অথবা, [math]\sin \theta=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=-\sin \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
বা, [math]\sin \theta=\sin \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6}[/math]
.: নির্ণেয় মান: [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #147 (ID: 705710)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: MSB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p \sin \theta+q \cos \theta=a[/math]

Options:
ক. একটি ত্রিভুজের তিনটি কোণের অনুপাত [math]5: 2: 7[/math]। বৃহত্তর কোণের বৃত্তীয় মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]a=\sqrt{p^{2}+q^{2}-r^{2}}[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]p \cos \theta=q \sin \theta \pm r[/math]
গ. [math]p=q=\sqrt{ } 3[/math] এবং [math]a=\sqrt{6}[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math]-এর মান নির্ণয় কর। যেখানে [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, একটি ত্রিভুজের তিনটি কোণের অনুপাত [math]5: 2: 7[/math]
মনে করি, ত্রিভুজের কোণত্রয় 5x 2x এবং 7x.আমরা জানি, ত্রিভুজের কোণত্রয়ের সমষ্টি 180° বা, [math]\pi[/math]
 রেডিয়ান।অর্থাৎ, [math]5 x+2 x+7 x=\pi \Rightarrow 14 x=\pi \quad \therefore x=\frac{\pi}{14}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 বৃহত্তম কোণ [math]=7 x=7 \times \frac{\pi}{14}[/math]
 রেডিয়ান [math]=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 রেডিয়ান [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]a=\sqrt{p^{2}+q^{2}-r^{2}}[/math]
এবং [math]p \sin \theta+q \cos \theta=a[/math]
অর্থাৎ [math]p \sin \theta+q \cos \theta=\sqrt{p^{2}+q^{2}-r^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow (p \sin \theta+q \cos \theta)^{2}=\left(\sqrt{p^{2}+q^{2}-r^{2}}\right)^{2}\\\Rightarrow p^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta+2 p q \sin \theta \cos \theta+q^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta=p^{2}+q^{2}\\\Rightarrow p^{2}-p^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta-2 p q \sin \theta \cos \theta+q^{2}-q^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta=r^{2}\\\Rightarrow p^{2}\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)-2 p q \sin \theta \cos \theta+q^{2}\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)=r^{2}\\\Rightarrow p^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta-2 p q \sin \theta \cos \theta+q^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta=r^{2}\\\Rightarrow (p \cos \theta)^{2}-2 \cdot p \cos \theta . q \sin \theta+(q \sin \theta)^{2}=r^{2}\\\Rightarrow (p \cos \theta-q \sin \theta)^{2}=r^{2}\\\Rightarrow p \cos \theta-q \sin \theta= \pm r\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{p} \cos \theta=\mathrm{q} \sin \theta \pm \mathrm{r}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]p=q=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 এবং [math]a=\sqrt{6}[/math]
 হলে উদ্দীপকের সমীকরণ হতে পাই,[math]\sqrt{3} \sin \theta+\sqrt{3} \cos \theta=\sqrt{6} ; 0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta+\cos \theta=\frac{\sqrt{6}}{\sqrt{3}} \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta+\cos \theta=\sqrt{2} \\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\sqrt{2}-\sin \theta \\\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta=(\sqrt{2}-\sin \theta)^{2} \\\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta=(\sqrt{2})^{2}-2 \cdot \sqrt{2} \cdot \sin \theta+\sin ^{2} \theta \\\Rightarrow 1-\sin ^{2} \theta=2-2 \sqrt{2} \sin \theta+\sin ^{2} \theta \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \theta-2 \sqrt{2} \sin \theta+1=0 \\\Rightarrow (\sqrt{2} \sin \theta)^{2}-2 \cdot \sqrt{2} \sin \theta \cdot 1+1^{2}=0 \\\Rightarrow (\sqrt{2} \sin \theta-1)^{2}=0 \Rightarrow \sqrt{2} \sin \theta-1=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{4}=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{4}\right) \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{4}=\sin \frac{3 \pi}{4} \therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{3 \pi}{4}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 হলে, [math]\sqrt{3} \sin \theta+\sqrt{3} \cos \theta=\sqrt{3} \sin \frac{\pi}{4}+\sqrt{3} \cos \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{2}}+\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{2}}=2 \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{2}}=\sqrt{6}[/math]
আবার, [math]\theta=\frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]
 হলে, [math]\sqrt{3} \sin \theta+\sqrt{3} \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3} \sin \frac{3 \pi}{4}+\sqrt{3} \cos \frac{3 \pi}{4}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{2}}-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{2}}=0 
eq \sqrt{6}[/math]
অর্থাৎ [math]\theta=\frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]
 প্রদত্ত সমীকরণকে সিদ্ধ করে না।[math]\therefore 0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]
 ব্যবধিতে [math]\theta[/math]
 এর মান [math]\frac{\pi}{4} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #148 (ID: 705711)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: MSB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\frac{\sin \theta-\cos \theta+1}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta-1}, B=\frac{\sin \theta+1}{\cos \theta}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\tan ^{2} \frac{7 \pi}{6}-\cos ^{2} \frac{5 \pi}{4}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]A^{2}-B^{2}=0[/math]
গ. [math]B=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর। যেখানে [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে,প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\tan ^{2} \frac{7 \pi}{6}-\cos ^{2} \frac{5 \pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\tan ^{2}\left(\frac{6 \pi+\pi}{6}\right)-\cos ^{2}\left(\frac{4 \pi+\pi}{4}\right)=\tan ^{2}\left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)-\cos ^{2}\left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{4}\right) \\=\left\{\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{6}\right)\right\}^{2}-\left\{-\cos \left(\frac{\pi}{4}\right)\right\}^{2}=\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\right)^{2}-\left(-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)^{2} \\=\frac{1}{3}-\frac{1}{2}=\frac{2-3}{6}=\frac{-1}{6} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{aligned}A & =\frac{\sin \theta-\cos \theta+1}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta-1} \\& =\frac{\cos \theta(\tan \theta-1+\sec \theta)}{\cos \theta(\tan \theta+1-\sec \theta)} \\& =\frac{(\tan \theta+\sec \theta)-\left(\sec ^{2} \theta-\tan ^{2} \theta\right)}{\tan \theta-\sec \theta+1} \\& =\frac{(\sec \theta+\tan \theta)-(\sec \theta+\tan \theta)(\sec \theta-\tan \theta)}{\tan \theta-\sec \theta+1} \\& =\frac{(\sec \theta+\tan \theta)(1-\sec \theta+\tan \theta)}{(1-\sec \theta+\tan \theta)} \\& =\sec \theta+\tan \theta \\& =\frac{1}{\cos \theta}+\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=\frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\left[\because B=\frac{\sin \theta+1}{\cos \theta}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A^{2}=B^{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A^{2}-B^{2}=0[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\begin{array}{l}B=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \theta+1}{\cos \theta}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}+\frac{1}{\cos \theta}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\\\Rightarrow \tan \theta+\sec \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \tan \theta+\sqrt{3} \sec \theta=1\\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \sec \theta=1-\sqrt{3} \tan \theta\\\Rightarrow (\sqrt{3} \sec \theta)^{2}=(1-\sqrt{3} \tan \theta)^{2}\\\Rightarrow 3 \sec ^{2} \theta=1-2 \sqrt{3} \tan \theta+3 \tan ^{2} \theta\\\Rightarrow 3\left(1+\tan ^{2} \theta\right)=1-2 \sqrt{3} \tan \theta+3 \tan ^{2} \theta\\\Rightarrow 3+3 \tan ^{2} \theta=1-2 \sqrt{3} \tan \theta+3 \tan ^{2} \theta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \sqrt{3} \tan \theta=1-3\\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\frac{-2}{2 \sqrt{3}} \Rightarrow \tan \theta=\frac{-1}{\sqrt{3}}\\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=-\tan \frac{\pi}{6} \Rightarrow \tan \theta=\tan \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\tan \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)\\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\tan \frac{5 \pi}{6}=\tan \frac{11 \pi}{6} \therefore \theta=\frac{5 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6}\end{array}[/math]
কিন্তু, [math]\theta=\frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
 গ্রহণযোগ্য নয়। কারণ,[math]\theta=\frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
 হলে, [math]B=\frac{\sin \frac{5 \pi}{6}+1}{\cos \frac{5 \pi}{6}}=\frac{\frac{1}{2}+1}{\frac{-\sqrt{3}}{2}}=-\sqrt{3} 
eq \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]
 ব্যবধিতে [math]\theta[/math]
 এর মান : [math]\frac{11 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #149 (ID: 705712)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta=a, \cos \theta+\sin \theta=x[/math] এবং [math]\cos \theta-\sin \theta=y[/math] তিনটি ত্রিকোণমিতিক সমীকরণ।

Options:
ক. [math]x = 1[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]\sin \theta-\cos \theta= \pm 1[/math]
খ. ১ম সমীকরণ হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\cos \theta=\frac{1-a^{2}}{1+a^{2}}[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{y+1}{x-1}=\frac{\sin \theta}{1-\cos \theta}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কএখানে, [math]x=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \theta+\sin \theta=1\\\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta+\sin ^{2} \theta+2 \sin \theta \cos \theta=1\\\Rightarrow 1+2 \sin \theta \cos \theta=1\\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta=0\\\Rightarrow -2 \sin \theta \cos \theta=0\\\Rightarrow 1-2 \sin \theta \cos \theta=1\\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta+\cos ^{2} \theta-2 \sin \theta \cos \theta=1\\\Rightarrow (\sin \theta-\cos \theta)^{2}=1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta-\cos \theta= \pm 1[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta=\mathbf{a}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sin \theta}-\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}=a \Rightarrow \frac{1-\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}=a\\\Rightarrow \frac{(1-\cos \theta)^{2}}{\sin ^{2} \theta}=a^{2} \Rightarrow \frac{(1-\cos \theta)^{2}}{1-\cos ^{2} \theta}=a^{2}\\\Rightarrow \frac{(1-\cos \theta)(1-\cos \theta)}{(1-\cos \theta)(1+\cos \theta)}=a^{2} \Rightarrow \frac{1-\cos \theta}{1+\cos \theta}=a^{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1-\cos \theta+1+\cos \theta}{1-\cos \theta-1-\cos \theta}=\frac{a^{2}+1}{a^{2}-1}[/math]
 [যোজন-বিয়োজন করে][math]\Rightarrow \frac{2}{-2 \cos \theta}=\frac{a^{2}+1}{a^{2}-1}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos \theta}=\frac{1+a^{2}}{1-a^{2}} \quad \therefore \cos \theta=\frac{1-a^{2}}{1+a^{2}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত [math]\\[/math]
 গবামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{y+1}{x-1}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\cos \theta-\sin \theta+1}{\cos \theta+\sin \theta-1}=\frac{\sin \theta\left(\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}-\frac{\sin \theta}{\sin \theta}+\frac{1}{\sin \theta}\right)}{\sin \theta\left(\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}+\frac{\sin \theta}{\sin \theta}-\frac{1}{\sin \theta}\right)} \\=\frac{(\cot \theta-1+\operatorname{cosec} \theta)}{(\cot \theta+1-\operatorname{cosec} \theta)}=\frac{\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta-1}{\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\left(\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta-\cot ^{2} \theta\right)} \\=\frac{\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta-1}{(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)(\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta)-(\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta)} \\=\frac{(\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta-1)}{(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)(\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta-1)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\frac{1}{\sin \theta}-\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}}=\frac{1}{\frac{1-\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}}=\frac{\sin \theta}{1-\cos \theta}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{y+1}{x-1}=\frac{\sin \theta}{1-\cos \theta}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:

Question #150 (ID: 705713)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x \sin \theta+y \cos \theta=z[/math] এবং [math]\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta-(2+\sqrt{2}) \operatorname{cosec} \theta+2 \sqrt{2}=0[/math] দুটি সমীকরণ।

Options:
ক. [math]40^{\circ} 55^{\prime} 54^{\prime \prime}[/math] কে রেডিয়ানে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. ১ম সমীকরণ হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]x \cos \theta-y \sin \theta= \pm \sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}-z^{2}}[/math]
গ. ২য় সমীকরণটি সমাধান কর যখন [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{aligned}40^{\circ} 55^{\prime} 54^{\prime \prime} & =40^{\circ}+\left(\frac{55}{60}\right)^{\circ}+\left(\frac{54}{60 \times 60}\right)^{\circ} \\& =\left(40+\frac{11}{12}+\frac{3}{200}\right)^{\circ} \\& =\left(\frac{40 \times 600+11 \times 50+3 \times 3}{600}\right)^{\circ} \\& =\left(\frac{24559}{600}\right)^{\circ}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{24559}{600} \times \frac{\pi}{180}\right)^{c}[/math]
 [ [math]\because 1^{\circ}=\frac{\pi}{180}[/math]
 রেডিয়ান][math]=\left(\frac{24559 \times 3.1416}{108000}\right)^{c}[/math]
 [math]=0.71439^{c}[/math]
 (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]x \sin \theta+y \cos \theta=z[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow (x \sin \theta+y \cos \theta)^{2}=z^{2}\\\Rightarrow x^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta+2 \cdot x \sin \theta \cdot y \cos \theta+y^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta=z^{2}\\\Rightarrow x^{2} \cdot\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)+2 x y \sin \theta \cos \theta+y^{2}\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)=z^{2}\\\Rightarrow x^{2}-x^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta+2 x y \sin \theta \cos \theta+y^{2}-y^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta=z^{2}\\\Rightarrow x^{2}+y^{2}-z^{2}=x^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta-2 \cdot x \cos \theta . y \sin \theta+y^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta\\\Rightarrow x^{2}+y^{2}-z^{2}=(x \cos \theta-y \sin \theta)^{2}\\\Rightarrow (x \cos \theta-y \sin \theta)^{2}=x^{2}+y^{2}-z^{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore x \cos \theta-y \sin \theta= \pm \sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}-z^{2}}[/math]
 (প্ৰমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,[math]\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta-(2+\sqrt{2}) \operatorname{cosec} \theta+2 \sqrt{2}=0;[/math]
 যখন [math]0<\theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta-2 \operatorname{cosec} \theta-\sqrt{2} \operatorname{cosec} \theta+2 \sqrt{2}=0 \\\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec} \theta(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-2)-\sqrt{2}(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-2)=0 \\\Rightarrow (\operatorname{cosec} \theta-2)(\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\sqrt{2})=0\end{array}[/math]
হয়, [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta-2=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec} \theta & =2 \\\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec} \theta & =\operatorname{cosec} \frac{\pi}{6} \\& =\operatorname{cosec}\left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
অথবা, [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\sqrt{2}=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec} \theta & =\sqrt{2} \\\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec} \theta & =\operatorname{cosec} \frac{\pi}{4} \\& =\operatorname{cosec}\left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{4}\right)\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]
 ব্যবধিতে প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটির সমাধান,[math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{3 \pi}{4}, \frac{5 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #151 (ID: 705714)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: DiB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\text { (i) } \cot \mathrm{A}+\operatorname{cosec} \mathrm{A}=m \text {. }[/math] [math]\text { (ii) }[/math] পৃথিবীর উপরের দুইটি স্থান পৃথিবীর কেন্দ্রে [math]5^{\circ} 6^{\prime} 36^{\prime \prime}[/math] কোণ উৎপন্ন করে।

Options:
ক. [math]\cos \left(-\frac{35 \pi}{6}\right)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\cos A=\frac{m^{2}-1}{m^{2}+1}[/math]
গ. পৃথিবীর ব্যাসার্ধ [math]6440[/math] কি.মি. হলে স্থানদ্বয়ের মধ্যবর্তী দূরত্ব নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\cos \left(-\frac{35 \pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\cos \left(\frac{35 \pi}{6}\right)[\because \cos (-\theta)=\cos \theta] \\=\cos \left(\frac{36 \pi-\pi}{6}\right) \\=\cos \left(6 \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \\=\cos \left(12 \times \frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\cos \frac{\pi}{6}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খসৃজনশীল ৯(খ) নং প্রশ্নের সমাধান দ্রষ্টব্য । পৃষ্ঠা-১৪৭ [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,স্থানদ্বয় দ্বারা পৃথিবীর কেন্দ্রে উৎপন্ন কোণ, [math]\theta=5^{\circ} 6^{\prime} 36^{\prime \prime}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=5^{\circ}+\left(\frac{6}{60}\right)^{\circ}+\left(\frac{36}{3600}\right)^{\circ} \\=(5+0.1+0.01)^{\circ} \\=5.11^{\circ}=\left(\frac{5.11 \times 3.1416}{180}\right)^{c}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=0.0892[/math]
 রেডিয়ান (প্রায়)এবং পৃথিবীর ব্যাসার্ধ, r = 6440 কি.মি.মনে করি, স্থানদ্বয়ের মধ্যবর্তী দূরত্ব = S[math]\therefore[/math]
 স্থানদ্বয়ের মধ্যবর্তী দূরত্ব, [math]S=r \theta[/math]
 [math]= 6440 × 0.0892[/math]
 কি.মি. [math]= 574.448[/math]
 কি.মি. (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #152 (ID: 705715)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: DiB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\cos \theta[/math] এবং [math]B=\sin \theta[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]0.5273[/math] রেডিয়ানকে ডিগ্রি এককে রূপান্তর কর।
খ. [math]XA - YB = Z,[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]X B+Y A= \pm \sqrt{X^{2}+Y^{2}-Z^{2}}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{1}{A^{2}}+\frac{B^{2}}{A^{2}}=\frac{5}{3}[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর, যেখানে [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত কোণ [math]=0.5273[/math]
 রেডিয়ান[math]=\left(0.5273 \times \frac{180}{\pi}\right)^{\circ}[/math]
 [ [math]\because 1[/math]
 রেডিয়ান [math]=\left(\frac{180^{\circ}}{\pi}\right)[/math]
][math]=\left(\frac{0.5273 \times 180}{3.1416}\right)^{\circ}=30.212^{\circ}[/math]
 (প্রায়)[math]\begin{array}{l}=30^{\circ}+(.212 \times 60)^{\prime}=30^{\circ} 12.72^{\prime} \\=30^{\circ} 12^{\prime}+(0.72 \times 60)^{\prime \prime}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=30^{\circ} 12^{\prime} 43.2^{\prime \prime}[/math]
 (প্রায়) [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{A}=\cos \theta, \mathrm{B}=\sin \theta[/math]
এবং [math]X A-Y B=Z[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow X \cos \theta-Y \sin \theta=Z[/math]
 [A ও B এর মান বসিয়ে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow (X \cos \theta-Y \sin \theta)^{2}=Z^{2}\\\Rightarrow X^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta-2 X \cos \theta . Y \sin \theta+Y^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta=Z^{2}\\\Rightarrow X^{2}\left(\mathrm{Y}-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)-2 X Y \sin \theta \cos \theta+Y^{2}\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)=Z^{2}\\\Rightarrow X^{2}-X^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta-2 X Y \sin \theta \cos \theta+Y^{2}-Y^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta=Z^{2}\\\Rightarrow -X^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta-2 X Y \sin \theta \cos \theta-Y^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta=Z^{2}-X^{2}-Y^{2}\\\Rightarrow X^{2} \sin ^{2} \theta+2 X Y \sin \theta \cos \theta+Y^{2} \cos ^{2} \theta=X^{2}+Y^{2}-Z^{2}\\\Rightarrow (X \sin \theta)^{2}+2(X \sin \theta)(Y \cos \theta)+(Y \cos \theta)^{2}=X^{2}+Y^{2}-Z^{2}\\\Rightarrow (X \sin \theta+Y \cos \theta)^{2}=X^{2}+Y^{2}-Z^{2}\\\Rightarrow X \sin \theta+Y \cos \theta= \pm \sqrt{X^{2}+Y^{2}-Z^{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left.X B+Y A= \pm \sqrt{X^{2}+Y^{2}-Z^{2}}\right)[/math]
 [A ও B এর মান বসিয়ে][math]\therefore \mathrm{XB}+\mathrm{YA}= \pm \sqrt{\mathrm{X}^{2}+\mathrm{Y}^{2}-\mathrm{Z}^{2}}[/math]
 (প্ৰমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\frac{1}{A^{2}}+\frac{B^{2}}{A^{2}}=\frac{5}{3};[/math]
 যেখানে, [math]0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos ^{2} \theta}+\frac{\sin ^{2} \theta}{\cos ^{2} \theta}=\frac{5}{3}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1+\sin ^{2} \theta}{\cos ^{2} \theta}=\frac{5}{3}\\\Rightarrow 3+3 \sin ^{2} \theta=5 \cos ^{2} \theta\\\Rightarrow 3+3 \sin ^{2} \theta=5\left(1-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)\\\Rightarrow 3+3 \sin ^{2} \theta=5-5 \sin ^{2} \theta\\\Rightarrow 8 \sin ^{2} \theta=2\\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{4}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta= \pm \frac{1}{2}[/math]
হয়, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \begin{array}{l} \sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{6} \\=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \frac{\pi}{6} \\=\sin \frac{5 \pi}{6} \\\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}\end{array}[/math]
অথবা, [math]\sin \theta=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=-\sin \frac{\pi}{6} \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \left(2 \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\sin \frac{7 \pi}{6}=\sin \frac{11 \pi}{6} \\\therefore \theta=\frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 0<\theta<2 \pi[/math]
 ব্যবধিতে [math]\theta[/math]
 এর মানসমূহ: [math]\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}, \frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
